 class BatchTaskDialog(QDialog):  # → 调用 BatchTaskDialog()
     """批量任务运行模式选择对话框"""

     # 任务类型映射：(标题, 动作描述)
     TASK_NAMES = {
         'export_fbx': ('批量导出FBX', '导出FBX'),
         'generate_preview': ('批量生成拍屏', '生成拍屏'),
         'upload_muse': ('批量上传到Muse', '上传到Muse')
     }

     def __init__(self, parent, task_type: str, anim_count: int, file_exists: bool = False):
         """
         Args:
             parent: 父窗口
             task_type: 任务类型 ('export_fbx', 'generate_preview', 'upload_muse')
             anim_count: 动画数量
             file_exists: 是否有文件已存在
         """
         super().__init__(parent)
         self.task_type = task_type
         self.anim_count = anim_count
         self.file_exists = file_exists
         self._result = None
         self._setup_ui()

     def _setup_ui(self):
         """初始化UI"""
         title, action = self.TASK_NAMES.get(self.task_type, ('批量任务', '处理'))
         self.setWindowTitle(title)
         self.setMinimumWidth(400)

         layout = QVBoxLayout(self)

         # 文本标签
         if self.task_type == 'upload_muse':
             # 上传Muse模式：只显示覆盖选项和确定/取消
             if self.anim_count == 1:
                 text = f"将为 1 个动画{action}"
             else:
                 text = f"将为 {self.anim_count} 个动画{action}"
             if self.file_exists:
                 text += "\n\n检测到部分动画已在Muse中存在"
             layout.addWidget(QLabel(text))
         else:
             # 其他模式：显示运行方式选项
             if self.anim_count == 1:
                 text = f"将为 1 个动画{action}\n\n运行方式：\n"
             else:
                 text = f"将为 {self.anim_count} 个动画{action}\n\n每个动画将在独立进程中运行\n\n运行方式：\n"
             layout.addWidget(QLabel(text))

         # 覆盖复选框
         self.overwrite_checkbox = QCheckBox("覆盖已存在文件")
         self.overwrite_checkbox.setChecked(False)
         if self.file_exists:
             self.overwrite_checkbox.setToolTip("勾选后将覆盖Muse中已存在的资产")
         layout.addWidget(self.overwrite_checkbox)

         # 按钮
         button_box = QDialogButtonBox()

         if self.task_type == 'upload_muse':
             # 上传Muse模式：只显示确定和取消按钮
             self.ok_btn = QPushButton("确定")
             self.cancel_btn = QPushButton("取消")
             button_box.addButton(self.ok_btn, QDialogButtonBox.AcceptRole)
             button_box.addButton(self.cancel_btn, QDialogButtonBox.RejectRole)
             self.ok_btn.clicked.connect(self._on_ok)
         else:
             # 其他模式：显示新窗口和后台运行按钮
             self.new_window_btn = QPushButton("新窗口（控制台日志）")
             self.background_btn = QPushButton("后台运行（日志文件）")
             self.cancel_btn = QPushButton("取消")
             button_box.addButton(self.new_window_btn, QDialogButtonBox.YesRole)
             button_box.addButton(self.background_btn, QDialogButtonBox.NoRole)
             button_box.addButton(self.cancel_btn, QDialogButtonBox.RejectRole)
             self.new_window_btn.clicked.connect(self._on_new_window)
             self.background_btn.clicked.connect(self._on_background)

         layout.addWidget(button_box)
         self.cancel_btn.clicked.connect(self.reject)

     def _on_ok(self):
         """确定按钮点击（上传Muse模式）"""
         self._result = {
             'run_mode': 'async',  # 异步模式
             'overwrite': self.overwrite_checkbox.isChecked()
         }
         self.accept()

     def _on_new_window(self):
         """新窗口按钮点击"""
         self._result = {
             'run_mode': 'new_window',
             'overwrite': self.overwrite_checkbox.isChecked()
         }
         self.accept()

     def _on_background(self):
         """后台运行按钮点击"""
         self._result = {
             'run_mode': 'background',
             'overwrite': self.overwrite_checkbox.isChecked()
         }
         self.accept()

     def get_result(self) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
         """获取对话框结果

         Returns:
             dict: {'run_mode': str, 'overwrite': bool} 或 None（取消）
         """
         return self._result

     @staticmethod
     def show_dialog(parent, task_type: str, anim_count: int, file_exists: bool = False) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
         """显示对话框并返回结果（静态方法，便于调用）

         Returns:
             dict: {'run_mode': str, 'overwrite': bool} 或 None（取消）
         """
         dialog = BatchTaskDialog(parent, task_type, anim_count, file_exists)
         if dialog.exec() == QDialog.Accepted:
             return dialog.get_result()
         return None


 class BatchTaskManager(QThread):  # → 调用 BatchTaskManager()
     """批量任务管理线程，控制并发数量并监控子进程状态"""

     log_message = Signal(str)
     status_updated = Signal(object, str, object)  # item, status, color
     finished_signal = Signal(int, int, int)  # completed, failed, total

     def __init__(
         self, 
         parent: 'AnimExportUI', 
         export_tasks: List[BatchTask], 
         max_concurrent: int, 
         task_config: Optional[Union[Dict[str, Any], TaskConfig]] = None
     ) -> None:
         super().__init__()
         self.parent = parent
         self.export_tasks = export_tasks
         self.max_concurrent = max_concurrent

         if isinstance(task_config, TaskConfig):
             self.task_config: Dict[str, Any] = {
                 'task_type': task_config.task_type,
                 'status_success': task_config.status_success,
                 'status_failed': task_config.status_failed,
                 'status_processing': task_config.status_processing,
                 'color_success': task_config.color_success,
                 'color_failed': task_config.color_failed,
                 'color_processing': task_config.color_processing,
                 'success_exit_code': task_config.success_exit_code,
                 'status_verification_failed': task_config.status_verification_failed,
                 'color_verification_failed': task_config.color_verification_failed,
                 'verification_failed_exit_code': task_config.verification_failed_exit_code,
                 'task_processor': task_config.task_processor,
                 'process_timeout': task_config.process_timeout,
                 'show_console': task_config.show_console,
             }
         else:
             self.task_config = task_config or {}

         self.running_processes: List[ProcessInfo] = []
         self.log_file_status: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]] = {}
         self.process_timeout: float = self.task_config.get('process_timeout', 300.0)

     def connect_signals(
         self, 
         log_callback: Callable[[str], None], 
         status_callback: Callable[[object, str, object], None], 
         finished_callback: Callable[[int, int, int], None]
     ) -> None:
         """连接信号到回调函数"""
         self.log_message.connect(log_callback)
         self.status_updated.connect(status_callback)
         self.finished_signal.connect(finished_callback)

     def _safe_update_status(self, item: Optional[QTreeWidgetItem], status: str, color: Any) -> None:
         """安全更新状态"""
         try:
             # 从第一个任务获取任务类型（所有任务类型相同）
             task_type = 'export_fbx'
             if self.export_tasks:
                 first_task = self.export_tasks[0]
                 if isinstance(first_task, PreviewTask):
                     task_type = 'generate_preview'
                 elif isinstance(first_task, UploadMuseTask):
                     task_type = 'upload_muse'
                 elif isinstance(first_task, ExportFbxTask):
                     task_type = 'export_fbx'
             elif isinstance(self.task_config, dict):
                 task_type = self.task_config.get('task_type', 'export_fbx')
             elif isinstance(self.task_config, TaskConfig):
                 task_type = self.task_config.task_type
             if task_type == 'generate_preview':
                 if item:
                     try:
                         if not hasattr(self.parent, 'data_center') or self.parent.data_center is None:
                             return
                         if not hasattr(self.parent.data_center, 'update_anim_preview_status'):
                             return
                         _ = item.data(0, Qt.UserRole)
                         self.parent.data_center.update_anim_preview_status(item, status, color)
                     except (RuntimeError, AttributeError):
                         traceback.print_exc()
             elif task_type == 'upload_muse':
                 if status in ['等待中...', '上传中...']:
                     try:
                         if item:
                             _ = item.data(0, Qt.UserRole)
                             item.setText(2, status)
                             item.setForeground(2, color)
                     except (RuntimeError, AttributeError):
                         pass
                 else:
                     if item:
                         try:
                             if not hasattr(self.parent, 'data_center') or self.parent.data_center is None:
                                 return
                             if not hasattr(self.parent.data_center, 'update_anim_muse_status'):
                                 return
                             _ = item.data(0, Qt.UserRole)
                             is_uploaded = (status == '已上传')
                             self.parent.data_center.update_anim_muse_status(item, is_uploaded)
                         except (RuntimeError, AttributeError):
                             traceback.print_exc()
             else:
                 if item:
                     try:
                         if not hasattr(self.parent, 'data_center') or self.parent.data_center is None:
                             return
                         if not hasattr(self.parent.data_center, 'update_anim_export_status'):
                             return

                         # 检查item是否在UI树中（虚拟item没有parent）
                         anim_data = item.data(0, Qt.UserRole)
                         ui_item = item

                         # 如果item不在UI树中（虚拟item），尝试查找UI树中对应的item
                         if not item.parent():
                             if anim_data:
                                 ui_item = self._find_item_by_anim_data(anim_data)
                                 if not ui_item:
                                     # 找不到UI树中的item，至少更新AnimData的状态
                                     if anim_data and isinstance(anim_data, AnimData):
                                         if status in ["已导出", "已存在", "成功"]:
                                             anim_data.is_exported = True
                                             if hasattr(anim_data, 'update_status'):
                                                 anim_data.update_status()
                                         elif status in ["导出失败", "验证失败", "失败"]:
                                             anim_data.is_exported = False
                                     return  # 无法更新UI，直接返回

                         # 使用找到的item更新UI
                         self.parent.data_center.update_anim_export_status(ui_item, status, color)
                     except (RuntimeError, AttributeError):
                         traceback.print_exc()
         except Exception:
             traceback.print_exc()

     def _find_item_by_fbx_path(self, fbx_path: str) -> Optional[QTreeWidgetItem]:
         """通过fbx_path在动画树中查找对应的item"""
         try:
             root = self.parent.ui.animTree.invisibleRootItem()
             for i in range(root.childCount()):
                 char_item = root.child(i)
                 for j in range(char_item.childCount()):
                     sk_item = char_item.child(j)
                     for k in range(sk_item.childCount()):
                         anim_item = sk_item.child(k)
                         try:
                             anim_data = anim_item.data(0, Qt.UserRole)
                             if anim_data and hasattr(anim_data, 'fbx_path') and anim_data.fbx_path == fbx_path:
                                 return anim_item
                         except:
                             continue
         except Exception as e:
             self.log_message.emit(f"⚠ 查找item时出错: {str(e)}")
         return None

     def _find_item_by_anim_data(self, target_anim_data) -> Optional[QTreeWidgetItem]:
         """通过AnimData在动画树中查找对应的item

         Args:
             target_anim_data: 目标AnimData对象

         Returns:
             QTreeWidgetItem对象，如果未找到则返回None
         """
         if not target_anim_data:
             return None

         try:
             # 使用anim_id映射进行O(1)查找
             if hasattr(target_anim_data, 'anim_id'):
                 anim_id = target_anim_data.anim_id
                 if anim_id:
                     return self.parent.data_center._anim_id_to_item_map.get(anim_id)
         except Exception as e:
             self.log_message.emit(f"⚠ 通过AnimData查找item时出错: {str(e)}")
         return None

     def _safe_update_anim_preview_status(self, item, status, color):
         """安全更新拍屏状态"""
         try:
             if not hasattr(self, 'parent') or self.parent is None:
                 return
             if not hasattr(self.parent, 'data_center') or self.parent.data_center is None:
                 return
             if not hasattr(self.parent.data_center, 'update_anim_preview_status'):
                 return

             # 如果item不在UI树中（虚拟item），尝试通过anim_data查找UI树中的item
             ui_item = item
             try:
                 # 检查item是否在UI树中（虚拟item没有parent）
                 if not item.parent():
                     # 尝试通过anim_data查找UI树中的item
                     anim_data = item.data(0, Qt.UserRole)
                     if anim_data and hasattr(anim_data, 'anim_id') and anim_data.anim_id:
                         ui_item = self.parent.data_center._anim_id_to_item_map.get(anim_data.anim_id)
                         if not ui_item:
                             # 如果找不到，回退到原始item（至少可以更新AnimData状态）
                             ui_item = item
                     else:
                         ui_item = item
             except (RuntimeError, AttributeError):
                 # item已被删除或无效，尝试通过anim_data查找
                 try:
                     anim_data = item.data(0, Qt.UserRole)
                     if anim_data and hasattr(anim_data, 'anim_id') and anim_data.anim_id:
                         ui_item = self.parent.data_center._anim_id_to_item_map.get(anim_data.anim_id)
                         if not ui_item:
                             ui_item = item
                     else:
                         ui_item = item
                 except:
                     ui_item = item

             self.parent.data_center.update_anim_preview_status(ui_item, status, color)
         except Exception:
             traceback.print_exc()

     def _get_item_from_task(self, task: BatchTask, task_type: str) -> Optional[QTreeWidgetItem]:
         """从任务对象中提取item"""
         try:
             if task_type == 'generate_preview':
                 if isinstance(task, PreviewTask):
                     return task.item
             elif task_type == 'upload_muse':
                 if isinstance(task, UploadMuseTask):
                     return task.item
             else:
                 if isinstance(task, ExportFbxTask):
                     return task.item
         except:
             return None
         return None

     def _kill_process_tree(self, process: subprocess.Popen) -> None:
         """Kill进程及其所有子进程（Windows平台）"""
         try:
             pid = process.pid
             if sys.platform == 'win32':
                 # 使用taskkill命令kill进程树（/T参数kill子进程）
                 try:
                     subprocess.run(
                         ['taskkill', '/F', '/T', '/PID', str(pid)],
                         timeout=10,
                         stdout=subprocess.DEVNULL,
                         stderr=subprocess.DEVNULL,
                         creationflags=subprocess.CREATE_NO_WINDOW if hasattr(subprocess, 'CREATE_NO_WINDOW') else 0
                     )
                 except (subprocess.TimeoutExpired, FileNotFoundError):
                     # 如果taskkill失败，回退到直接kill
                     try:
                         process.kill()
                     except:
                         pass
             else:
                 # 非Windows平台，直接kill进程（子进程通常会自动结束）
                 try:
                     process.kill()
                 except:
                     pass

             # 等待进程结束
             try:
                 process.wait(timeout=5)
             except:
                 pass
         except Exception:
             # 如果所有方法都失败，至少尝试kill主进程
             try:
                 process.kill()
             except:
                 pass

     def _handle_process_timeout(self, info: ProcessInfo, elapsed_time: float) -> None:
         """处理进程超时"""
         import time as time
         # Kill进程树（包括modellib.exe等子进程）
         self._kill_process_tree(info.process)

         # 等待文件句柄释放（Windows系统可能需要更多时间）
         if info.log_path and os.path.exists(info.log_path):
             timeout_message = (
                 f"\n\n========================================\n"
                 f"进程超时强制结束\n"
                 f"运行时间: {int(elapsed_time)}秒\n"
                 f"超时限制: {int(self.process_timeout)}秒\n"
                 f"结束时间: {time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}\n"
                 f"========================================\n"
             )

             # 重试机制：尝试多次写入日志文件
             max_retries = 5
             retry_delay = 0.5
             for attempt in range(max_retries):
                 try:
                     # 等待文件句柄释放
                     if attempt > 0:
                         time.sleep(retry_delay * attempt)

                     with open(info.log_path, 'a', encoding='utf-8', errors='replace') as f:
                         f.write(timeout_message)
                     break  # 成功写入，退出重试循环
                 except (PermissionError, IOError) as e:
                     if attempt == max_retries - 1:
                         # 最后一次尝试失败，记录警告但不影响主流程
                         self.log_message.emit(f"⚠ 写入超时日志失败: 文件被占用，无法写入（已重试{max_retries}次）")
                     continue
                 except Exception as e:
                     self.log_message.emit(f"⚠ 写入超时日志失败: {str(e)}")
                     break

         # 从第一个任务获取任务类型（所有任务类型相同）
         task_type = 'export_fbx'
         if self.export_tasks:
             first_task = self.export_tasks[0]
             if isinstance(first_task, PreviewTask):
                 task_type = 'generate_preview'
             elif isinstance(first_task, UploadMuseTask):
                 task_type = 'upload_muse'
             elif isinstance(first_task, ExportFbxTask):
                 task_type = 'export_fbx'

         status_timeout = f"超时({int(elapsed_time)}s)"
         color_timeout = QColor(255, 165, 0)
         self._update_status_by_task_type(task_type, info.item, status_timeout, color_timeout, info.anim_name)

         if info.log_path and info.log_path in self.log_file_status:
             del self.log_file_status[info.log_path]

     def _update_status_by_task_type(self, task_type: str, item, status: str, color, anim_name: str = "") -> None:
         """根据任务类型更新状态"""
         if task_type == 'generate_preview':
             self._safe_update_anim_preview_status(item, status, color)
         elif task_type == 'upload_muse':
             if item:
                 try:
                     item.setText(2, status)
                     item.setForeground(2, color)
                 except:
                     pass
         else:
             if item:
                 try:
                     if hasattr(self.parent, 'data_center') and self.parent.data_center is not None:
                         self.parent.data_center.update_anim_export_status(item, status, color)
                 except Exception as e:
                     self.log_message.emit(f"⚠ 更新状态失败: {anim_name} - {str(e)}")

     def _calculate_preview_progress(self, log_path: str) -> Tuple[int, bool, int]:
         """计算拍屏进度，返回 (进度百分比, 日志是否更新, 行数)"""
         current_time = time.time()
         file_mtime = os.path.getmtime(log_path)

         with open(log_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8', errors='replace') as f:
             lines = f.readlines()
             line_count = len(lines)

         log_updated = False
         if log_path not in self.log_file_status:
             self.log_file_status[log_path] = {
                 'last_mtime': file_mtime,
                 'last_line_count': line_count,
                 'last_update_time': current_time
             }
             log_updated = True
         else:
             status = self.log_file_status[log_path]
             if file_mtime > status['last_mtime'] or line_count > status['last_line_count']:
                 status['last_mtime'] = file_mtime
                 status['last_line_count'] = line_count
                 status['last_update_time'] = current_time
                 log_updated = True

         progress = 0
         log_content = ''.join(lines).lower()

         if 'start rendering' in log_content or '开始渲染' in log_content:
             progress = 30
         if 'rendering frame' in log_content or '渲染帧' in log_content:
             frame_matches = re.findall(r'frame\s+(\d+)', log_content, re.IGNORECASE)
             if frame_matches:
                 max_frame = max([int(f) for f in frame_matches if f.isdigit()])
                 progress = min(30 + int((max_frame / 100) * 50), 80)
             else:
                 progress = 50
         if 'saved' in log_content or '保存' in log_content or 'complete' in log_content or '完成' in log_content:
             progress = 90

         if progress == 0:
             if line_count < 50:
                 progress = 10
             elif line_count < 200:
                 progress = 30
             elif line_count < 500:
                 progress = 50
             elif line_count < 1000:
                 progress = 70
             else:
                 progress = 85

         return progress, log_updated, line_count

     def _check_log_stale(self, log_path: str, anim_name: str, item: Optional[QTreeWidgetItem], status_processing: str) -> bool:
         """检查日志是否长时间未更新，返回是否异常"""
         if log_path in self.log_file_status:
             status = self.log_file_status[log_path]
             time_since_update = time.time() - status['last_update_time']
             if time_since_update >= 20:
                 status_error = f"{status_processing} ⚠异常(日志{int(time_since_update)}s未更新)"
                 color_error = QColor(255, 165, 0)
                 lprint.warning(f"[拍屏异常] {anim_name}: 日志文件超过{int(time_since_update)}秒未更新")
                 self.parent.data_center.update_anim_preview_status(item, status_error, color_error)
                 return True
         return False

     def _handle_process_completed(self, info: ProcessInfo) -> Tuple[int, int]:
         """处理已完成的进程，返回 (completed_delta, failed_delta)"""
         if info.log_path and info.log_path in self.log_file_status:
             del self.log_file_status[info.log_path]

         # 从第一个任务获取配置（所有任务配置相同）
         config = None
         if self.export_tasks:
             first_task = self.export_tasks[0]
             if isinstance(first_task, ExportFbxTask) and first_task.config:
                 config = first_task.config
             elif isinstance(first_task, PreviewTask) and first_task.config:
                 config = first_task.config
             elif isinstance(first_task, UploadMuseTask) and first_task.config:
                 config = first_task.config

         # 如果没有配置，使用后备配置
         if not config:
             if isinstance(self.task_config, TaskConfig):
                 config = self.task_config
             else:
                 # 从字典创建默认配置
                 task_type = self.task_config.get('task_type', 'export_fbx')
                 config = TaskConfig(
                     task_type=task_type,
                     status_success=self.task_config.get('status_success', '成功'),
                     status_failed=self.task_config.get('status_failed', '失败'),
                     status_processing=self.task_config.get('status_processing', '处理中...'),
                     color_success=self.task_config.get('color_success', Qt.green),
                     color_failed=self.task_config.get('color_failed', Qt.red),
                     color_processing=self.task_config.get('color_processing', Qt.blue),
                     success_exit_code=self.task_config.get('success_exit_code', 0),
                     status_verification_failed=self.task_config.get('status_verification_failed'),
                     color_verification_failed=self.task_config.get('color_verification_failed'),
                     verification_failed_exit_code=self.task_config.get('verification_failed_exit_code'),
                     process_timeout=self.task_config.get('process_timeout', 300.0),
                     show_console=self.task_config.get('show_console', False),
                 )

         success_exit_code = config.success_exit_code
         verification_failed_exit_code = config.verification_failed_exit_code
         status_success = config.status_success
         status_failed = config.status_failed
         status_verification_failed = config.status_verification_failed or '验证失败'
         color_success = config.color_success
         color_failed = config.color_failed
         color_verification_failed = config.color_verification_failed or Qt.yellow
         color_output_missing = QColor(255, 100, 0)  # 橙红色：输出文件缺失
         task_type = config.task_type

         if info.process.returncode == success_exit_code:
             # 退出码成功，但需要验证输出文件是否存在
             outputs_ok, missing_files = info.verify_outputs()

             if not outputs_ok:
                 # 日志存在但输出文件不存在 → 表格列显示为失败
                 # 详细缺失文件列表仍写到日志窗口
                 if task_type == 'upload_muse':
                     self.parent.data_center.update_anim_muse_status(info.item, False)
                 elif task_type == 'generate_preview':
                     self._safe_update_anim_preview_status(info.item, status_failed, color_failed)
                 else:
                     self.status_updated.emit(info.item, status_failed, color_failed)

                 missing_names = [os.path.basename(f) for f in missing_files]
                 self.log_message.emit(f"✗ 输出文件缺失: {info.anim_name} - {', '.join(missing_names)}")
                 return 0, 1

             # 输出文件验证通过
             if task_type == 'upload_muse':
                 self.parent.data_center.update_anim_muse_status(info.item, True)
             elif task_type == 'generate_preview':
                 self._safe_update_anim_preview_status(info.item, status_success, color_success)
             else:
                 self.status_updated.emit(info.item, status_success, color_success)
             self.log_message.emit(f"✓ {status_success}: {info.anim_name}")
             return 1, 0
         elif verification_failed_exit_code and info.process.returncode == verification_failed_exit_code:
             if task_type == 'generate_preview':
                 self._safe_update_anim_preview_status(info.item, status_verification_failed, color_verification_failed)
             else:
                 self.status_updated.emit(info.item, status_verification_failed, color_verification_failed)
             self.log_message.emit(f"✗ {status_verification_failed}: {info.anim_name} (退出码: {info.process.returncode})")
             return 0, 1
         else:
             if task_type == 'upload_muse':
                 self.parent.data_center.update_anim_muse_status(info.item, False)
             elif task_type == 'generate_preview':
                 self._safe_update_anim_preview_status(info.item, status_failed, color_failed)
             else:
                 self.status_updated.emit(info.item, status_failed, color_failed)
             self.log_message.emit(f"✗ {status_failed}: {info.anim_name} (退出码: {info.process.returncode})")
             return 0, 1

     def _update_preview_progress(self, info: ProcessInfo) -> None:
         """更新拍屏任务的进度"""
         # 从第一个任务获取配置
         config = None
         if self.export_tasks:
             first_task = self.export_tasks[0]
             if isinstance(first_task, PreviewTask) and first_task.config:
                 config = first_task.config

         if config:
             status_processing = config.status_processing
             color_processing = config.color_processing
         else:
             status_processing = self.task_config.get('status_processing', '处理中...') if isinstance(self.task_config, dict) else '处理中...'
             color_processing = self.task_config.get('color_processing', Qt.blue) if isinstance(self.task_config, dict) else Qt.blue

         if not info.show_console and info.log_path and os.path.exists(info.log_path):
             try:
                 progress, log_updated, line_count = self._calculate_preview_progress(info.log_path)

                 if not log_updated:
                     self._check_log_stale(info.log_path, info.anim_name, info.item, status_processing)

                 if log_updated or info.log_path not in self.log_file_status:
                     status_with_progress = f"{status_processing} {progress}%"
                     self._safe_update_anim_preview_status(info.item, status_with_progress, color_processing)
             except Exception:
                 traceback.print_exc()
                 self._safe_update_anim_preview_status(info.item, status_processing, color_processing)
         else:
             if not info.show_console:
                 lprint.warning(f"[拍屏进度] {info.anim_name}: {status_processing} (日志文件不存在: {info.log_path})")
             self._safe_update_anim_preview_status(info.item, status_processing, color_processing)

     def _start_process(self, script_path: str, show_console: bool) -> 'subprocess.Popen[bytes]':
         """启动脚本进程（支持.bat和.ps1文件）"""
         script_dir = os.path.dirname(script_path)
         env = os.environ.copy()

         # 判断是否为PowerShell脚本
         is_ps1 = script_path.lower().endswith('.ps1')

         if is_ps1:
             # 直接启动PowerShell脚本
             if show_console:
                 # 新窗口模式：创建新的可见PowerShell窗口
                 return subprocess.Popen(
                     ['powershell.exe', '-ExecutionPolicy', 'Bypass', '-File', script_path],
                     shell=False, cwd=script_dir,
                     creationflags=subprocess.CREATE_NEW_CONSOLE | subprocess.CREATE_NEW_PROCESS_GROUP
                 )
             else:
                 # 后台模式：创建隐藏的PowerShell窗口
                 startupinfo = subprocess.STARTUPINFO()
                 startupinfo.dwFlags |= subprocess.STARTF_USESHOWWINDOW
                 startupinfo.wShowWindow = subprocess.SW_HIDE
                 return subprocess.Popen(
                     ['powershell.exe', '-ExecutionPolicy', 'Bypass', '-File', script_path],
                     shell=False, cwd=script_dir, startupinfo=startupinfo,
                     creationflags=subprocess.CREATE_NEW_CONSOLE | subprocess.CREATE_NEW_PROCESS_GROUP
                 )
         else:
             # 原有的bat文件启动方式
             if show_console:
                 return subprocess.Popen(
                     [script_path], shell=False, cwd=script_dir,
                     creationflags=subprocess.CREATE_NEW_CONSOLE | subprocess.CREATE_NEW_PROCESS_GROUP
                 )
             else:
                 startupinfo = subprocess.STARTUPINFO()
                 startupinfo.dwFlags |= subprocess.STARTF_USESHOWWINDOW
                 startupinfo.wShowWindow = subprocess.SW_HIDE
                 return subprocess.Popen([script_path], shell=True, startupinfo=startupinfo,
                 creationflags=subprocess.CREATE_NEW_CONSOLE | subprocess.CREATE_NEW_PROCESS_GROUP)

     def _start_preview_task(self, task: PreviewTask, task_index: int) -> Union[ProcessInfo, Literal["skip"]]:
         """启动拍屏任务，返回进程信息或 'skip'"""
         anim_data = task.anim_data
         fbx_ske_ani_path = task.input_fbx_path
         anim_name = task.anim_name
         settings = task.settings
         item = task.item
         expected_outputs = task.output_files

         if not all([fbx_ske_ani_path, anim_name, settings, item]):
             raise Exception(f"任务参数不完整: {anim_name}")

         # 从任务配置中获取状态和颜色
         config = task.config or TaskConfig(task_type='generate_preview', status_success='已拍屏', status_failed='拍屏失败', status_processing='拍屏中...', color_success=QColor(100, 255, 100), color_failed=QColor(255, 100, 100), color_processing=QColor(100, 200, 255), success_exit_code=3)
         status_processing = config.status_processing
         color_processing = config.color_processing

         if anim_data and hasattr(anim_data, 'mp4_path') and anim_data.mp4_path and os.path.exists(anim_data.mp4_path):
             if not settings.get('overwrite_playblast', False):
                 self._safe_update_anim_preview_status(item, "已存在", Qt.gray)
                 self.log_message.emit(f"⊘ 跳过（已存在）: {anim_name}")
                 return "skip"
             self.log_message.emit(f"⚠ 覆盖已存在文件: {anim_name}")

         self._safe_update_anim_preview_status(item, status_processing, color_processing)
         script_path, log_path = self.parent._generate_preview_bat(fbx_ske_ani_path, anim_name, settings, anim_data=anim_data)

         if not script_path or not os.path.exists(script_path):
             raise Exception(f"脚本文件生成失败: {script_path}")

         show_console = config.show_console
         process = self._start_process(script_path, show_console)

         if log_path:
             self.log_message.emit(f"📝 日志文件: {log_path}")

         return ProcessInfo(
             process=process,
             item=item,
             anim_name=anim_name,
             fbx_path=task.output_fbx_ske_mesh_ani_path,
             log_path=log_path,
             enable_log=settings.get('enable_log', '0'),
             show_console=show_console,
             start_time=time.time(),
             expected_outputs=expected_outputs
         )

     def _start_upload_task(self, task: UploadMuseTask, task_index: int) -> Optional[ProcessInfo]:
         """启动Muse上传任务"""
         fbx_path = task.fbx_path
         mp4_path = task.mp4_path
         gif_path = task.gif_path
         anim_name = task.anim_name
         custom_tags = task.custom_tags
         hierarchy_template = task.hierarchy_template
         config_context = task.config_context
         category_root = task.category_root
         item = task.item
         enable_log = task.enable_log

         # 从任务配置中获取状态和颜色
         config = task.config or TaskConfig(task_type='upload_muse', status_success='已上传', status_failed='上传失败', status_processing='上传中...', color_success=QColor(100, 255, 100), color_failed=QColor(255, 100, 100), color_processing=QColor(100, 200, 255), success_exit_code=3)
         status_processing = config.status_processing
         color_processing = config.color_processing

         self.status_updated.emit(item, status_processing, color_processing)
         # 从task.anim_data获取anim_data
         anim_data = task.anim_data
         bat_path, log_path = self.parent._generate_single_upload_impl(
             fbx_path, mp4_path, gif_path, anim_name, custom_tags,
             hierarchy_template, config_context, category_root, enable_log,
             anim_data=anim_data
         )

         if not bat_path or not os.path.exists(bat_path):
             raise Exception(f"批处理文件生成失败: {bat_path}")

         show_console = config.show_console
         process = self._start_process(bat_path, show_console)

         if log_path:
             self.log_message.emit(f"📝 日志文件: {log_path}")

         return ProcessInfo(
             process=process,
             item=item,
             anim_name=anim_name,
             fbx_path=fbx_path,
             log_path=log_path,
             enable_log=enable_log,
             show_console=show_console,
             start_time=time.time(),
             expected_outputs=[]
         )

     def _start_export_task(self, task: ExportFbxTask, task_index: int) -> Union[ProcessInfo, Literal["skip"]]:
         """启动FBX导出任务"""
         anim_data = task.anim_data
         anim_res = task.anim_res
         sk_name = task.sk_name
         anim_name = task.anim_name
         char_name = task.char_name
         item = task.item
         expected_outputs = task.output_files

         # 从任务配置中获取状态和颜色
         config = task.config or TaskConfig(task_type='export_fbx', status_success='已导出', status_failed='导出失败', status_processing='导出中...', color_success=QColor(100, 255, 100), color_failed=QColor(255, 100, 100), color_processing=QColor(100, 200, 255), success_exit_code=3)
         status_processing = config.status_processing
         color_processing = config.color_processing

         if anim_data.fbx_path and os.path.exists(anim_data.fbx_path):
             # 从任务对象中获取覆盖设置
             if not task.overwrite_fbx:
                 self.status_updated.emit(item, "已存在", Qt.gray)
                 self.log_message.emit(f"⊘ 跳过（已存在）: {anim_name}")
                 return "skip"
             self.log_message.emit(f"⚠ 覆盖已存在文件: {anim_name}")

         self.status_updated.emit(item, status_processing, color_processing)

         # 将 show_console 配置保存到 anim_data，以便批处理模板使用
         if not hasattr(anim_data, 'export_fbx_config'):
             anim_data.export_fbx_config = {}
         anim_data.export_fbx_config['show_console'] = config.show_console

         temp_dir = os.environ.get("TEMP", os.environ.get("TMP", ""))
         if not temp_dir:
             raise ValueError("无法获取临时目录路径（TEMP和TMP环境变量都未设置）")

         modellib_bat_dir = os.path.join(temp_dir, "H72Messiah_AL_temp", "batch_fbx_export")

         try:
             lprint(f"[DEBUG] 开始生成批处理文件: 骨骼={sk_name}, 动画={anim_name}, 目录={modellib_bat_dir}")
             bat_path, log_path = self.parent.generate_modellib_batch_file(
                 sk_name, anim_res, modellib_bat_dir, bat_prefix="batch_export", use_models=False,
                 char_name=char_name, task_index=task_index, anim_data=anim_data
             )
             lprint(f"[DEBUG] 批处理文件生成成功: bat_path={bat_path}, log_path={log_path}")
         except Exception as e:
             error_msg = f"生成批处理文件失败: {anim_name} - {str(e)}"
             lprint(error_msg)
             import traceback
             traceback.print_exc()
             raise Exception(error_msg)

         # 验证返回的路径
         if not bat_path:
             raise ValueError(f"批处理文件路径为空: {anim_name}")

         # 规范化路径
         bat_path = os.path.normpath(os.path.abspath(bat_path))
         log_path = os.path.normpath(os.path.abspath(log_path)) if log_path else None

         # 验证文件是否存在
         if not os.path.exists(bat_path):
             raise IOError(f"批处理文件不存在: {bat_path} (动画: {anim_name})")

         # 验证文件大小
         try:
             file_size = os.path.getsize(bat_path)
             if file_size == 0:
                 raise IOError(f"批处理文件大小为0: {bat_path}")
         except Exception as e:
             raise IOError(f"无法验证批处理文件: {bat_path} - {str(e)}")

         # 记录bat文件路径
         self.log_message.emit(f"📄 批处理文件: {bat_path}")

         show_console = config.show_console
         process = self._start_process(bat_path, show_console)

         if log_path:
             self.log_message.emit(f"📝 日志文件: {log_path}")

         return ProcessInfo(
             process=process,
             item=item,
             anim_name=anim_name,
             fbx_path=task.output_fbx_path,
             log_path=log_path,
             enable_log='1',
             show_console=show_console,
             start_time=time.time(),
             expected_outputs=expected_outputs
         )

     def _start_single_task(self, task: BatchTask, task_index: int) -> Tuple[Union[ProcessInfo, Literal["skip"]], str]:
         """启动单个任务，返回 (进程信息或'skip', 动画名称)"""
         # 从任务对象获取任务类型
         if isinstance(task, PreviewTask):
             task_type = 'generate_preview'
         elif isinstance(task, UploadMuseTask):
             task_type = 'upload_muse'
         else:
             task_type = 'export_fbx'

         if task_type == 'generate_preview':
             if not isinstance(task, PreviewTask):
                 raise TypeError(f"任务类型错误: 期望 PreviewTask，实际 {type(task)}")
             anim_name = task.anim_name
             result = self._start_preview_task(task, task_index)
         elif task_type == 'upload_muse':
             if not isinstance(task, UploadMuseTask):
                 raise TypeError(f"任务类型错误: 期望 UploadMuseTask，实际 {type(task)}")
             anim_name = task.anim_name
             result = self._start_upload_task(task, task_index)
         else:
             if not isinstance(task, ExportFbxTask):
                 raise TypeError(f"任务类型错误: 期望 ExportFbxTask，实际 {type(task)}")
             anim_name = task.anim_name
             result = self._start_export_task(task, task_index)

         return result, anim_name

     def run(self) -> None:
         """运行批量任务管理器，监控子进程状态"""
         # 记录开始时间
         self._batch_start_time = time.time()

         task_index = 0
         total_tasks = len(self.export_tasks)
         completed_count = 0
         failed_count = 0

         # 从第一个任务获取配置（所有任务配置相同）
         task_type = 'export_fbx'
         if self.export_tasks:
             first_task = self.export_tasks[0]
             if isinstance(first_task, ExportFbxTask) and first_task.config:
                 task_type = first_task.config.task_type
             elif isinstance(first_task, PreviewTask) and first_task.config:
                 task_type = first_task.config.task_type
             elif isinstance(first_task, UploadMuseTask) and first_task.config:
                 task_type = first_task.config.task_type
             else:
                 task_type = self.task_config.get('task_type', 'export_fbx') if isinstance(self.task_config, dict) else (self.task_config.task_type if isinstance(self.task_config, TaskConfig) else 'export_fbx')

         status_waiting_map = {'generate_preview': '等待拍屏', 'upload_muse': '等待上传'}
         status_waiting = status_waiting_map.get(task_type, '等待导出')
         color_waiting = QColor(180, 180, 180)

         for task in self.export_tasks:
             item = self._get_item_from_task(task, task_type)
             if item:
                 self._update_status_by_task_type(task_type, item, status_waiting, color_waiting)

         while task_index < total_tasks or self.running_processes:
             still_running: List[ProcessInfo] = []
             current_time = time.time()

             for info in self.running_processes:
                 elapsed_time = current_time - info.start_time

                 if info.process.poll() is None and elapsed_time > self.process_timeout:
                     self._handle_process_timeout(info, elapsed_time)
                     failed_count += 1
                     log_file_info = f" (日志: {info.log_path})" if info.log_path and os.path.exists(info.log_path) else ""
                     self.log_message.emit(f"✗ 超时强制结束 ({int(elapsed_time)}s): {info.anim_name}{log_file_info}")
                     continue

                 if info.process.poll() is None:
                     if task_type == 'generate_preview':
                         self._update_preview_progress(info)
                     still_running.append(info)
                 else:
                     c_delta, f_delta = self._handle_process_completed(info)
                     completed_count += c_delta
                     failed_count += f_delta
                     # 更新状态栏显示进度和耗时
                     elapsed_time = time.time() - self._batch_start_time
                     progress_text = f"进度: {completed_count + failed_count}/{total_tasks} | 成功: {completed_count} | 失败: {failed_count} | 已耗时: {elapsed_time:.1f}秒"
                     self.log_message.emit(f"📊 {progress_text}")

             self.running_processes = still_running

             while task_index < total_tasks and len(self.running_processes) < self.max_concurrent:
                 task = self.export_tasks[task_index]
                 task_index += 1

                 try:
                     result, anim_name = self._start_single_task(task, task_index)

                     if result == "skip":
                         completed_count += 1
                         continue

                     if result:
                         self.running_processes.append(result)
                         log_info = f" [日志: {result.log_path}]" if result.log_path else ""
                         elapsed_time = time.time() - getattr(self, '_batch_start_time', time.time())
                         self.log_message.emit(f"✓ 已启动 ({task_index}/{total_tasks}): {anim_name} [并发: {len(self.running_processes)}/{self.max_concurrent}] [超时: {int(self.process_timeout)}s] [已耗时: {elapsed_time:.1f}s]{log_info}")

                 except Exception as e:
                     traceback.print_exc()
                     failed_count += 1
                     status_failed = self.task_config.get('status_failed', '失败')
                     color_failed = self.task_config.get('color_failed', Qt.red)
                     self.log_message.emit(f"✗ 启动失败: {str(e)}")
                     item = self._get_item_from_task(task, task_type)
                     if item:
                         self.status_updated.emit(item, status_failed, color_failed)

             time.sleep(2)

         self.finished_signal.emit(completed_count, failed_count, total_tasks)


 class MuseCheckThread(QThread):  # → 调用 MuseCheckThread()
     """Muse状态检查线程，异步检查动画是否已上传到Muse

     检查所有页的动画，并直接修改AnimData的muse_status字段
     使用category_ids进行精确搜索
     """

     check_progress = Signal(object, str, bool)  # (anim_data, anim_name, exists)
     check_complete = Signal(int)  # total_count

     def __init__(self, parent: 'AnimExportUI', check_queue: List):
         super().__init__(parent)
         self.parent_widget = parent
         self.check_queue = check_queue  # [(anim_data, anim_name, anim_res), ...]
         self._category_tree_cache = None  # 缓存分类树

     def run(self):
         """在后台线程中运行检查（使用异步支持高并发）"""
         from muse_python_api import MuseClient
         from muse_python_api.enums import MuseAssetType
         from collections import defaultdict

         email = self.parent_widget.ui.museUserEdit.text()
         organization_id = self.parent_widget.ui.museLibEdit.text()
         asset_type_str = self.parent_widget.ui.museAssetTypeEdit.currentText()

         try:
             asset_type = getattr(MuseAssetType, asset_type_str, MuseAssetType.simpleaction)
         except:
             asset_type = MuseAssetType.simpleaction

         # 创建客户端实例
         client = MuseClient(email=email, organization_id=organization_id, asset_type=asset_type)

         def _looks_like_category_id(x: str) -> bool:
             return bool(x) and str(x).isdigit()

         # 1) 按 leaf category_id 分组（避免“每条动画一请求”）
         #    category_ids 预期形如 ['123456']；没有则进入 fallback
         category_to_items: dict[str, list[tuple]] = defaultdict(list)
         fallback_items: list[tuple] = []
         for anim_data, anim_name, anim_res in self.check_queue:
             ids = getattr(anim_data, "category_ids", None)
             leaf_id = None
             if isinstance(ids, list) and ids:
                 leaf_id = str(ids[0]).strip()
                 if not _looks_like_category_id(leaf_id):
                     leaf_id = None
             if leaf_id:
                 category_to_items[leaf_id].append((anim_data, anim_name, anim_res))
             else:
                 fallback_items.append((anim_data, anim_name, anim_res))

         total_count = len(self.check_queue)
         processed = 0
         lprint(f"Muse状态检查：按分类分组 {len(category_to_items)} 组，fallback {len(fallback_items)} 个动画")

         # 2) 每个分类一次性分页拉取全部资产，然后本地比对 anim_name
         #    注意：leaf_id应该是骨骼层级的ID，返回的资产应该都是该骨骼层级下的
         for leaf_id, items in category_to_items.items():
             try:
                 lprint(f"[批量查询] 开始查询分类: category_id={leaf_id}, 包含 {len(items)} 个动画")
                 page_size = 500  # 增大分页大小，减少API调用次数
                 page_number = 1
                 name_set: set[str] = set()
                 total_records = 0
                 api_call_count = 0

                 # 验证：确保leaf_id确实是骨骼层级ID（通过检查items中的骨骼是否一致）
                 skeleton_names_in_group = set()
                 for anim_data, anim_name, anim_res in items:
                     skeleton_name = getattr(anim_data, 'skeleton_name', '')
                     if skeleton_name:
                         skeleton_names_in_group.add(skeleton_name)

                 skeleton_count = len(skeleton_names_in_group)
                 max_display_count = skeleton_count * page_size if skeleton_count > 0 else 0
                 lprint(f"[批量查询] 涉及 {skeleton_count} 个骨骼，每页 {page_size}，最多显示 {max_display_count}")

                 if len(skeleton_names_in_group) > 1:
                     lprint(f"[批量查询] 警告：category_id={leaf_id} 包含多个骨骼: {skeleton_names_in_group}，可能存在骨骼层级混淆")

                 # 使用分页查询获取所有资产
                 while True:
                     api_call_count += 1
                     lprint(f"[批量查询] API请求 #{api_call_count}: category_ids=[{leaf_id}], page_size={page_size}, page_number={page_number}")
                     result = client.search_assets(category_ids=[leaf_id], page_size=page_size, page_number=page_number)
                     records = (result or {}).get("records") or []
                     total_records += len(records)

                     # 第一页时获取总数
                     if page_number == 1:
                         real_total = (result or {}).get("real_total_count") or len(records)
                         lprint(f"[批量查询] 返回结果: 本页 {len(records)} 个资产，实际总数 {real_total}")
                     else:
                         lprint(f"[批量查询] 返回结果: 第{page_number}页 {len(records)} 个资产，累计 {total_records} 个资产")

                     # 收集资产名称（骨骼层级查询，返回的资产应该都是该骨骼层级下的）
                     for r in records:
                         n = r.get("asset_name") or r.get("name")
                         if n:
                             # 可选：验证资产的category_ids是否包含leaf_id（双重验证）
                             asset_categories = r.get("categories", [])
                             if isinstance(asset_categories, list):
                                 category_ids_str = [str(cat) for cat in asset_categories if cat]
                                 if leaf_id in category_ids_str:
                                     name_set.add(str(n))
                                 else:
                                     lprint(f"[批量查询] 警告：资产 {n} 的category_ids不包含查询的leaf_id={leaf_id}，跳过")
                             else:
                                 # 如果没有categories字段，回退到只匹配名称（可能不准确）
                                 name_set.add(str(n))

                     # 检查是否继续查询下一页
                     if len(records) < page_size:
                         lprint(f"[批量查询] 已到最后一页 (records={len(records)} < page_size={page_size})")
                         break

                     page_number += 1

                 lprint(f"[批量查询] 查询完成: category_id={leaf_id}，共调用 {api_call_count} 次API，总共找到 {len(name_set)} 个唯一资产名称（骨骼层级）")

                 matched_count = 0
                 unmatched_count = 0
                 for anim_data, anim_name, anim_res in items:
                     exists = bool(anim_name) and (anim_name in name_set)
                     object.__setattr__(anim_data, "muse_status", "已上传" if exists else "未上传")
                     object.__setattr__(anim_data, "is_uploaded", exists)
                     processed += 1
                     self.check_progress.emit(anim_data, anim_name, exists)

                     if exists:
                         matched_count += 1
                     else:
                         unmatched_count += 1

                 lprint(f"[批量查询] 匹配结果: category_id={leaf_id}，已上传={matched_count}, 未上传={unmatched_count}，共调用 {api_call_count} 次API")
             except Exception as e:
                 lprint(f"[批量查询] 检查Muse分类失败: category_id={leaf_id} - {str(e)}")
                 import traceback
                 traceback.print_exc()
                 for anim_data, anim_name, anim_res in items:
                     object.__setattr__(anim_data, "muse_status", "未检查")
                     processed += 1
                     self.check_progress.emit(anim_data, anim_name, None)

         # 3) fallback：批量查询层级ID列表下的所有角色，然后本地匹配动画名称
         #    使用分类树解析层级ID，然后批量查询
         if fallback_items:
             # 获取层级模板
             hierarchy_template = "{char_name}/{skeleton_name}"  # 默认模板
             try:
                 if hasattr(self.parent_widget, 'ui') and hasattr(self.parent_widget.ui, 'muse_upload_dir'):
                     hierarchy_template = self.parent_widget.ui.muse_upload_dir.currentText() or hierarchy_template
             except:
                 pass

             lprint(f"[批量查询] 层级模板: {hierarchy_template}")
             lprint(f"[批量查询] fallback动画总数: {len(fallback_items)}")

             # 尝试获取分类树并构建层级ID映射
             category_tree = None
             hierarchy_id_map = {}
             try:
                 # 等待分类树加载完成（最多等待5秒）
                 if hasattr(self.parent_widget, 'data_center') and self.parent_widget.data_center:
                     # 确保分类树已开始加载
                     self.parent_widget.data_center.ensure_muse_category_tree_cached()

                     # 等待分类树加载完成
                     import time
                     max_wait = 5.0
                     wait_interval = 0.1
                     waited = 0.0
                     while waited < max_wait:
                         category_tree = getattr(self.parent_widget.data_center, '_muse_category_tree', None)
                         if category_tree:
                             break
                         time.sleep(wait_interval)
                         waited += wait_interval

                     if category_tree:
                         # 构建层级路径到ID的映射
                         def build_hierarchy_map(tree_node, path_list=None):
                             """递归构建层级路径到ID的映射"""
                             if path_list is None:
                                 path_list = []

                             node_id = tree_node.get('id')
                             node_name_multil = tree_node.get('name_multil', {}) or {}
                             node_name = node_name_multil.get('zh_CN', '') or node_name_multil.get('en_US', '') or tree_node.get('name', '')

                             current_path = path_list + [node_name] if node_name else path_list

                             if node_id and current_path:
                                 # 构建路径字符串（如 "svn,Char,角色名,骨骼名"）
                                 path_str = ','.join(current_path)
                                 hierarchy_id_map[path_str] = str(node_id)

                             children = tree_node.get('children', [])
                             for child in children:
                                 build_hierarchy_map(child, current_path)

                         if isinstance(category_tree, list):
                             for root_node in category_tree:
                                 build_hierarchy_map(root_node)
                         elif isinstance(category_tree, dict):
                             build_hierarchy_map(category_tree)

                         lprint(f"[批量查询] 构建层级ID映射成功，共 {len(hierarchy_id_map)} 个层级")
                         # 打印所有层级路径和ID的映射（用于调试）
                         for path_str, hid in sorted(hierarchy_id_map.items()):
                             lprint(f"  [{path_str}] -> {hid}")
                     else:
                         lprint(f"[批量查询] 警告：分类树未加载完成（等待{waited:.1f}秒后超时）")
             except Exception as e:
                 lprint(f"[批量查询] 构建层级ID映射失败: {str(e)}")
                 import traceback
                 traceback.print_exc()

             # 按层级ID分组fallback动画
             hierarchy_to_items: dict[str, list[tuple]] = defaultdict(list)
             name_only_items: list[tuple] = []

             # 统计分组信息
             char_group_stats = defaultdict(int)  # 统计每个角色组的动画数量
             skeleton_group_stats = defaultdict(int)  # 统计每个骨骼组的动画数量

             for anim_data, anim_name, anim_res in fallback_items:
                 if not anim_name:
                     object.__setattr__(anim_data, "muse_status", "未检查")
                     processed += 1
                     self.check_progress.emit(anim_data, anim_name, None)
                     continue

                 # 从AnimData获取角色名和骨骼名
                 char_name = getattr(anim_data, 'character_name', '')
                 skeleton_name = getattr(anim_data, 'skeleton_name', '')

                 if char_name and skeleton_name:
                     # 使用层级模板构建层级路径（如 "角色名/骨骼名"）
                     hierarchy_path = hierarchy_template.replace("{char_name}", char_name).replace("{skeleton_name}", skeleton_name)
                     # 转换为完整层级路径（如 "svn,Char,角色名,骨骼名"）
                     category_path = f"svn,Char,{hierarchy_path.replace('/', ',')}"
                     # 角色层级路径（如 "svn,Char,角色名"）
                     char_category_path = f"svn,Char,{char_name}"

                     # 查找对应的层级ID
                     hierarchy_id = hierarchy_id_map.get(category_path)
                     matched_type = None
                     if hierarchy_id and _looks_like_category_id(hierarchy_id):
                         hierarchy_to_items[hierarchy_id].append((anim_data, anim_name, anim_res))
                         matched_type = "骨骼层级"
                         skeleton_group_stats[f"{char_name}/{skeleton_name}"] += 1
                     else:
                         # 如果找不到精确匹配，尝试查找父层级（角色层级）
                         char_hierarchy_id = hierarchy_id_map.get(char_category_path)
                         if char_hierarchy_id and _looks_like_category_id(char_hierarchy_id):
                             hierarchy_to_items[char_hierarchy_id].append((anim_data, anim_name, anim_res))
                             matched_type = "角色层级"
                             char_group_stats[char_name] += 1
                         else:
                             name_only_items.append((anim_data, anim_name, anim_res))
                             matched_type = "未匹配"
                 else:
                     name_only_items.append((anim_data, anim_name, anim_res))

             # 打印详细的分组统计信息
             lprint(f"[批量查询] ========== 分组结果 ==========")
             lprint(f"[批量查询] 按层级ID分组: {len(hierarchy_to_items)} 组")
             lprint(f"[批量查询] 无法分组: {len(name_only_items)} 个动画")

             # 打印每个层级组的详细信息
             for idx, (hierarchy_id, items) in enumerate(hierarchy_to_items.items(), 1):
                 # 查找这个层级ID对应的路径名称
                 path_name = "未知"
                 for path_str, hid in hierarchy_id_map.items():
                     if hid == hierarchy_id:
                         path_name = path_str
                         break

                 # 统计这个组中的角色和骨骼
                 chars_in_group = set()
                 skeletons_in_group = defaultdict(int)
                 for anim_data, anim_name, anim_res in items:
                     char_name = getattr(anim_data, 'character_name', '')
                     skeleton_name = getattr(anim_data, 'skeleton_name', '')
                     if char_name:
                         chars_in_group.add(char_name)
                     if skeleton_name:
                         sk_key = f"{char_name}/{skeleton_name}"
                         skeletons_in_group[sk_key] += 1

                 # 判断是角色层级还是骨骼层级
                 path_parts = path_name.split(',')
                 if len(path_parts) >= 4:
                     group_type = "骨骼层级"
                     group_desc = f"角色={path_parts[2]}, 骨骼={path_parts[3]}"
                 elif len(path_parts) >= 3:
                     group_type = "角色层级"
                     group_desc = f"角色={path_parts[2]}"
                 else:
                     group_type = "其他层级"
                     group_desc = path_name

                 page_size = 500  # 每页骨骼数
                 max_display_count = len(skeletons_in_group) * page_size  # 最多显示数量 = 骨骼数 × 每页数

                 lprint(f"[批量查询] 组{idx}: [{hierarchy_id}]")
                 lprint(f"[批量查询]   - 类型: {group_type}")
                 lprint(f"[批量查询]   - 路径: {path_name}")
                 lprint(f"[批量查询]   - 描述: {group_desc}")
                 lprint(f"[批量查询]   - 包含 {len(items)} 个动画")
                 lprint(f"[批量查询]   - 涉及 {len(chars_in_group)} 个角色: {', '.join(sorted(chars_in_group))}")
                 lprint(f"[批量查询]   - 涉及 {len(skeletons_in_group)} 个骨骼组合，每页 {page_size}，最多显示 {max_display_count}:")
                 for sk_name, count in sorted(skeletons_in_group.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True):
                     lprint(f"[批量查询]     * {sk_name}: {count} 个动画，每页 {page_size}，最多显示 {page_size}")

             # 批量查询每个层级ID下的所有资产（一次性获取所有页，然后统一匹配）
             for hierarchy_id, items in hierarchy_to_items.items():
                 # 查找层级名称
                 path_name = "未知"
                 for path_str, hid in hierarchy_id_map.items():
                     if hid == hierarchy_id:
                         path_name = path_str
                         break

                 try:
                     lprint(f"[批量查询] 开始查询层级: hierarchy_id={hierarchy_id}, path={path_name}, 包含 {len(items)} 个动画")

                     # 判断是角色层级还是骨骼层级
                     path_parts = path_name.split(',')
                     is_skeleton_level = len(path_parts) >= 4  # 骨骼层级：svn,Char,角色名,骨骼名

                     # 如果是角色层级，需要构建每个骨骼的层级ID映射，用于验证资产的骨骼层级
                     skeleton_hierarchy_ids = {}
                     if not is_skeleton_level:
                         # 角色层级：需要为每个动画找到其骨骼的层级ID
                         for anim_data, anim_name, anim_res in items:
                             char_name = getattr(anim_data, 'character_name', '')
                             skeleton_name = getattr(anim_data, 'skeleton_name', '')
                             if char_name and skeleton_name:
                                 # 构建骨骼层级路径
                                 hierarchy_path = hierarchy_template.replace("{char_name}", char_name).replace("{skeleton_name}", skeleton_name)
                                 skeleton_category_path = f"svn,Char,{hierarchy_path.replace('/', ',')}"
                                 skeleton_hid = hierarchy_id_map.get(skeleton_category_path)
                                 if skeleton_hid and _looks_like_category_id(skeleton_hid):
                                     sk_key = f"{char_name}/{skeleton_name}"
                                     if sk_key not in skeleton_hierarchy_ids:
                                         skeleton_hierarchy_ids[sk_key] = skeleton_hid

                     # 一次性获取该层级下的所有资产（循环分页直到获取完所有数据）
                     page_size = 500  # 增大分页大小，减少API调用次数
                     page_number = 1
                     name_set: set[str] = set()  # 骨骼层级：只存储动画名称
                     asset_map: dict[str, dict] = {}  # 角色层级：存储动画名称 -> 资产记录（包含category_ids）
                     total_records = 0
                     api_call_count = 0

                     while True:
                         api_call_count += 1
                         lprint(f"[批量查询] API请求 #{api_call_count}: category_ids=[{hierarchy_id}], page_size={page_size}, page_number={page_number}")
                         result = client.search_assets(category_ids=[hierarchy_id], page_size=page_size, page_number=page_number)

                         records = (result or {}).get("records") or []
                         total_records += len(records)

                         lprint(f"[批量查询] API返回 #{api_call_count}: 本页 {len(records)} 个资产，累计 {total_records} 个资产")

                         # 收集资产信息
                         for r in records:
                             n = r.get("asset_name") or r.get("name")
                             if n:
                                 if is_skeleton_level:
                                     # 骨骼层级：只存储动画名称（已经限定了骨骼层级）
                                     name_set.add(str(n))
                                 else:
                                     # 角色层级：存储完整资产记录（用于验证骨骼层级）
                                     asset_categories = r.get("categories", [])
                                     if isinstance(asset_categories, list):
                                         asset_map[str(n)] = {
                                             "name": str(n),
                                             "categories": [str(cat) for cat in asset_categories if cat]
                                         }
                                     else:
                                         asset_map[str(n)] = {
                                             "name": str(n),
                                             "categories": []
                                         }

                         # 检查是否继续查询下一页
                         if len(records) < page_size:
                             lprint(f"[批量查询] 已到最后一页 (records={len(records)} < page_size={page_size})")
                             break

                         page_number += 1

                     if is_skeleton_level:
                         lprint(f"[批量查询] 查询完成: 共调用 {api_call_count} 次API，总共找到 {len(name_set)} 个唯一资产名称（骨骼层级）")
                     else:
                         lprint(f"[批量查询] 查询完成: 共调用 {api_call_count} 次API，总共找到 {len(asset_map)} 个资产（角色层级，需要验证骨骼层级）")

                     # 一次性匹配所有动画（使用已获取的完整数据集）
                     matched_count = 0
                     unmatched_count = 0
                     for anim_data, anim_name, anim_res in items:
                         exists = False

                         if is_skeleton_level:
                             # 骨骼层级：只匹配动画名称（已经限定了骨骼层级）
                             exists = bool(anim_name) and (anim_name in name_set)
                         else:
                             # 角色层级：需要验证资产的category_ids是否包含该骨骼的层级ID
                             if anim_name and anim_name in asset_map:
                                 asset = asset_map[anim_name]
                                 asset_categories = asset.get("categories", [])

                                 # 获取该动画所属骨骼的层级ID
                                 char_name = getattr(anim_data, 'character_name', '')
                                 skeleton_name = getattr(anim_data, 'skeleton_name', '')
                                 if char_name and skeleton_name:
                                     sk_key = f"{char_name}/{skeleton_name}"
                                     skeleton_hid = skeleton_hierarchy_ids.get(sk_key)

                                     if skeleton_hid:
                                         # 验证资产的category_ids是否包含该骨骼的层级ID
                                         exists = skeleton_hid in asset_categories
                                     else:
                                         # 如果找不到骨骼层级ID，回退到只匹配动画名称（可能不准确）
                                         exists = True
                                         lprint(f"[批量查询] 警告：动画 {anim_name} ({sk_key}) 找不到骨骼层级ID，使用名称匹配（可能不准确）")
                                 else:
                                     # 如果没有角色名和骨骼名，回退到只匹配动画名称
                                     exists = True
                         object.__setattr__(anim_data, "muse_status", "已上传" if exists else "未上传")
                         object.__setattr__(anim_data, "is_uploaded", exists)
                         processed += 1
                         self.check_progress.emit(anim_data, anim_name, exists)

                         if exists:
                             matched_count += 1
                         else:
                             unmatched_count += 1

                     lprint(f"[批量查询] 匹配结果: 已上传={matched_count}, 未上传={unmatched_count}")
                     lprint(f"[批量查询] 批量查询层级成功: hierarchy_id={hierarchy_id} ({path_name})，找到 {len(name_set) if is_skeleton_level else len(asset_map)} 个资产，匹配 {len(items)} 个动画，共调用 {api_call_count} 次API")
                 except Exception as e:
                     lprint(f"[批量查询] 批量检查Muse层级失败: hierarchy_id={hierarchy_id} ({path_name}) - {str(e)}")
                     import traceback
                     traceback.print_exc()
                     # 失败时回退到逐个查询
                     for anim_data, anim_name, anim_res in items:
                         name_only_items.append((anim_data, anim_name, anim_res))

             # 对于仍然无法批量查询的动画，按名称逐个查询（最后的后备方案）
             # 注意：需要验证资产的骨骼层级，避免不同骨骼的同名动画被错误匹配
             if name_only_items:
                 lprint(f"开始逐个查询 {len(name_only_items)} 个动画的Muse状态（需要验证骨骼层级）")

             for anim_data, anim_name, anim_res in name_only_items:
                 try:
                     # 获取该动画所属骨骼的层级ID（用于验证）
                     char_name = getattr(anim_data, 'character_name', '')
                     skeleton_name = getattr(anim_data, 'skeleton_name', '')
                     skeleton_hid = None

                     if char_name and skeleton_name:
                         # 构建骨骼层级路径
                         hierarchy_path = hierarchy_template.replace("{char_name}", char_name).replace("{skeleton_name}", skeleton_name)
                         skeleton_category_path = f"svn,Char,{hierarchy_path.replace('/', ',')}"
                         skeleton_hid = hierarchy_id_map.get(skeleton_category_path)
                         if skeleton_hid and not _looks_like_category_id(skeleton_hid):
                             skeleton_hid = None

                     result = client.search_assets(asset_name=anim_name, page_size=60)
                     records = (result or {}).get("records") or []

                     exists = False
                     if records:
                         if skeleton_hid:
                             # 验证是否有资产的category_ids包含该骨骼的层级ID
                             for r in records:
                                 asset_categories = r.get("categories", [])
                                 if isinstance(asset_categories, list):
                                     category_ids_str = [str(cat) for cat in asset_categories if cat]
                                     if skeleton_hid in category_ids_str:
                                         exists = True
                                         break

                             if not exists:
                                 lprint(f"[逐个查询] 动画 {anim_name} ({char_name}/{skeleton_name}) 找到同名资产，但都不属于该骨骼层级（skeleton_hid={skeleton_hid}）")
                         else:
                             # 如果找不到骨骼层级ID，回退到只匹配动画名称（可能不准确）
                             exists = True
                             lprint(f"[逐个查询] 警告：动画 {anim_name} ({char_name}/{skeleton_name}) 找不到骨骼层级ID，使用名称匹配（可能不准确，不同骨骼的同名动画可能被错误匹配）")
                     else:
                         exists = False

                     object.__setattr__(anim_data, "muse_status", "已上传" if exists else "未上传")
                     object.__setattr__(anim_data, "is_uploaded", exists)
                     processed += 1
                     self.check_progress.emit(anim_data, anim_name, exists)
                 except Exception as e:
                     lprint(f"检查Muse状态失败: {anim_name} - {str(e)}")
                     object.__setattr__(anim_data, "muse_status", "未检查")
                     processed += 1
                     self.check_progress.emit(anim_data, anim_name, None)

         self.check_complete.emit(total_count)


 class FileSizeCheckThread(QThread):  # → 调用 FileSizeCheckThread()
     """文件大小检查线程"""

     size_progress = Signal(object, str)  # (item, size_text)
     size_complete = Signal(int)  # total_count

     def __init__(self, parent: 'AnimExportUI', file_size_queue: List):
         super().__init__(parent)
         self.parent_widget = parent
         self.file_size_queue = file_size_queue

     def run(self):
         """在后台线程中运行文件大小检查"""
         from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed

         def get_file_size(anim_item, anim_path):
             """获取单个文件大小"""
             try:
                 if os.path.exists(anim_path):
                     size_bytes = os.path.getsize(anim_path)
                     if size_bytes < 1024:
                         size_text = f"{size_bytes} B"
                     elif size_bytes < 1024 * 1024:
                         size_text = f"{size_bytes / 1024:.2f} KB"
                     else:
                         size_text = f"{size_bytes / (1024 * 1024):.2f} MB"
                     return anim_item, size_text
                 else:
                     return anim_item, "文件不存在"
             except Exception as e:
                 return anim_item, f"错误: {str(e)}"

         with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=8) as executor:
             future_to_item = {
                 executor.submit(get_file_size, item, path): item
                 for item, path in self.file_size_queue
             }

             for future in as_completed(future_to_item):
                 try:
                     anim_item, size_text = future.result()
                     self.size_progress.emit(anim_item, size_text)
                 except Exception as e:
                     lprint(f"获取文件大小异常: {str(e)}")

         self.size_complete.emit(len(self.file_size_queue))


 class ScanWorker(QThread):  # → 调用 ScanWorker()
     """扫描工作线程 - 按角色-骨骼结构扫描"""

     progress = Signal(int, int)  # current, total
     character_found = Signal(str, object)  # char_name, char_data (CharacterData对象)
     finished = Signal(int)  # total count

     def __init__(self, char_dir, engine_root, scan_limit=20, skeleton_limit=10):
         super().__init__()
         self.char_dir = char_dir
         self.engine_root = engine_root
         self.scan_limit = scan_limit
         self.skeleton_limit = skeleton_limit

     def scan_skeleton_anims(self, skeleton_info: SkeletonInfo) -> tuple[str, SkeletonData]:
         """扫描单个骨骼的动画文件（用于多线程）

         Args:
             skeleton_info: 骨骼扫描信息

         Returns:
             (骨骼名称, 骨骼数据)
         """
         # 从.skeleton文件中读取动画的res字段信息（结构体列表）
         anim_res_list = utils.get_anim_res_from_skeleton(skeleton_info.skeleton_path)

         # 直接从.skeleton文件中读取的动画列表创建AnimData
         anims: list[AnimData] = []

         # 使用UI中设置的引擎目录构建Package目录
         package_dir = os.path.join(self.engine_root, "Package")

         # 遍历anim_res_list，直接从.skeleton文件创建AnimData
         char_name = skeleton_info.character_name

         # 计算骨骼文件所在目录相对于Package的路径，用于拼接相对路径动画
         # 例如：skeleton_dir = .../Package/Char/b_05_old/b_01_char_jiangwulang_man
         #       skeleton_rel_prefix = "Char/b_05_old/b_01_char_jiangwulang_man/"
         skeleton_dir_normalized = skeleton_info.skeleton_dir.replace("\\", "/")
         package_dir_normalized = package_dir.replace("\\", "/")
         if skeleton_dir_normalized.startswith(package_dir_normalized):
             skeleton_rel_prefix = skeleton_dir_normalized[len(package_dir_normalized):].strip("/") + "/"
         else:
             # 兜底：从skeleton_dir中提取Char/之后的部分
             char_idx = skeleton_dir_normalized.find("Char/")
             if char_idx != -1:
                 skeleton_rel_prefix = skeleton_dir_normalized[char_idx:].strip("/") + "/"
             else:
                 skeleton_rel_prefix = f"Char/{char_name}/"

         for anim_res_info in anim_res_list:
             anim_name = anim_res_info.name
             res_path = anim_res_info.res

             # 步骤1: 规范化res_path为相对于Package的路径
             # res_path可能的格式：
             # - Char/a_05_old/a_05_char_common_monster/ani/xxx.anim (跨角色引用/retarget，直接使用)
             # - /ani/A.anim (相对于骨骼文件所在目录的路径)
             normalized_res_path = res_path.replace("\\", "/")

             if normalized_res_path.startswith("Char/"):
                 # 跨角色引用（retarget），已经是相对于Package的完整路径，直接使用
                 anim_rel_path = normalized_res_path
             else:
                 # 相对路径（如 /ani/A.anim），相对于骨骼文件所在目录
                 # 拼接为：骨骼目录相对路径 + 去掉开头斜杠的res路径
                 clean_path = normalized_res_path.lstrip("/.")
                 anim_rel_path = f"{skeleton_rel_prefix}{clean_path}"

             # 步骤2: 基于规范化后的路径生成muse_tag和完整路径
             # 使用规范化后的路径初始化muse_tags
             anim_data = AnimData(
                 path="",  # 先设置为空，后面统一设置
                 res=res_path,  # 保留原始res字段
                 name=anim_name,
                 skeleton_name=skeleton_info.skeleton_name,
                 character_name=char_name,
                 skeleton_path=skeleton_info.skeleton_path
             )

             # 使用规范化后的路径初始化muse_tags
             normalized_tags = [anim_name, anim_rel_path, skeleton_info.skeleton_path]
             anim_data._initialize_muse_tags(normalized_tags)

             # 步骤3: 基于规范化路径生成完整的anim_path
             # anim_rel_path已经是相对于Package的路径（如 "Char/b_01_char_male/1_base/b_death.anim"）
             # 需要与package_dir拼接
             anim_path = os.path.join(package_dir, *anim_rel_path.split("/"))
             anim_path = os.path.normpath(anim_path)

             # 更新AnimData的path字段
             object.__setattr__(anim_data, 'path', anim_path)

             # 设置日志文件路径（先不检查存在性，在后台线程中检查）
             export_fbx_log_path = anim_data.export_fbx_log_file
             preview_log_path = anim_data.preview_log_file
             upload_muse_log_path = anim_data.upload_muse_log_file

             object.__setattr__(anim_data, 'export_fbx_log_path', export_fbx_log_path)
             object.__setattr__(anim_data, 'preview_log_path', preview_log_path)
             object.__setattr__(anim_data, 'upload_muse_log_path', upload_muse_log_path)
             # 先设置为False，后台线程会检查并更新
             object.__setattr__(anim_data, 'export_fbx_log_exists', False)
             object.__setattr__(anim_data, 'preview_log_exists', False)
             object.__setattr__(anim_data, 'upload_muse_log_exists', False)

             anims.append(anim_data)

         return skeleton_info.skeleton_name, SkeletonData(path=skeleton_info.skeleton_path, anims=anims)

     def run(self):
         try:
             import time as _time
             from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed

             _t_total = _time.time()

             # 第一步：扫描角色目录（Char下的一级目录）
             lprint(f"[扫描] 第一步：扫描角色目录 {self.char_dir}")
             _t0 = _time.time()
             # 非角色目录黑名单
             _SKIP_DIRS = {'.svn', 'anim_tag'}
             character_dirs = []
             with os.scandir(self.char_dir) as entries:
                 for entry in entries:
                     if entry.is_dir(follow_symlinks=False) and not entry.name.startswith('.') and entry.name not in _SKIP_DIRS:
                         character_dirs.append((entry.name, entry.path))
             lprint(f"[扫描] 第一步完成：找到 {len(character_dirs)} 个角色目录，耗时 {_time.time() - _t0:.2f}s")

             # 第二步：收集所有骨骼信息（快速遍历，不读取动画）
             lprint(f"[扫描] 第二步：收集骨骼信息...")
             _t1 = _time.time()
             all_skeleton_infos = []
             char_skeleton_map = {}  # {char_name: [skeleton_infos]}

             for idx, (char_name, char_path) in enumerate(character_dirs):
                 _t_char = _time.time()
                 skeleton_infos = []
                 skeleton_count = 0

                 # 快速扫描角色目录下的所有.skeleton文件（限制数量）
                 for root, dirs, files in os.walk(char_path):
                     for file in files:
                         if file.endswith(".skeleton"):
                             # 检查是否达到骨骼数量限制
                             if skeleton_count >= self.skeleton_limit:
