                                 break

                             skeleton_path = os.path.join(root, file)
                             skeleton_name = os.path.splitext(file)[0]
                             skeleton_dir = root

                             # 创建SkeletonInfo对象
                             skeleton_info = SkeletonInfo(
                                 skeleton_dir=skeleton_dir,
                                 skeleton_path=skeleton_path,
                                 skeleton_name=skeleton_name,
                                 character_name=char_name
                             )
                             skeleton_infos.append(skeleton_info)
                             all_skeleton_infos.append((char_name, skeleton_info))
                             skeleton_count += 1

                     # 如果已达到限制，退出外层循环
                     if skeleton_count >= self.skeleton_limit:
                         break

                 if skeleton_infos:
                     char_skeleton_map[char_name] = skeleton_infos
                 print(f"[扫描] 角色 [{idx+1}/{len(character_dirs)}] {char_name}: {skeleton_count} 个骨骼，耗时 {_time.time() - _t_char:.2f}s")

             # 汇总无骨骼的角色
             no_skeleton_chars = [name for name, _ in character_dirs if name not in char_skeleton_map]
             if no_skeleton_chars:
                 print(f"[扫描] 以下 {len(no_skeleton_chars)} 个角色目录无.skeleton文件，已跳过: {', '.join(no_skeleton_chars)}")
             print(f"[扫描] 第二步完成：{len(character_dirs)} 个角色目录，{len(char_skeleton_map)} 个有骨骼，共 {len(all_skeleton_infos)} 个骨骼，耗时 {_time.time() - _t1:.2f}s")

             # 第三步：使用线程池并行扫描所有骨骼的动画
             lprint(f"[扫描] 第三步：并行解析 {len(all_skeleton_infos)} 个骨骼的动画（线程数=8）...")
             _t2 = _time.time()
             skeleton_results = {}  # {(char_name, sk_name): sk_data}
             total_skeletons = len(all_skeleton_infos)
             total_characters = len(character_dirs)
             processed_count = 0
             processed_chars = set()

             with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=8) as executor:
                 # 提交所有骨骼扫描任务
                 future_to_info = {
                     executor.submit(self.scan_skeleton_anims, info): (char_name, info)
                     for char_name, info in all_skeleton_infos
                 }
                 lprint(f"[扫描] 已提交 {len(future_to_info)} 个骨骼扫描任务")

                 # 处理完成的任务
                 for future in as_completed(future_to_info):
                     try:
                         char_name, skeleton_info = future_to_info[future]
                         sk_name, sk_data = future.result()
                         skeleton_results[(char_name, sk_name)] = sk_data
                         processed_count += 1
                         processed_chars.add(char_name)
                         anim_count = len(sk_data.anims) if sk_data else 0
                         print(f"[扫描] 骨骼 [{processed_count}/{total_skeletons}] {char_name}/{sk_name}: {anim_count} 个动画")
                         # 显示角色进度而不是骨骼进度
                         self.progress.emit(len(processed_chars), total_characters)
                     except Exception as e:
                         char_name, skeleton_info = future_to_info[future]
                         processed_count += 1
                         print(f"[扫描] 骨骼 [{processed_count}/{total_skeletons}] {char_name}/{skeleton_info.skeleton_name} 异常: {str(e)}")

             print(f"[扫描] 第三步完成：解析 {processed_count} 个骨骼，耗时 {_time.time() - _t2:.2f}s")

             # 将进度设为100%（无骨骼的角色不会在第三步中被计入进度）
             self.progress.emit(total_characters, total_characters)

             # 第四步：按角色组织数据并发送信号（包括无骨骼的角色）
             lprint(f"[扫描] 第四步：组织角色数据并发送信号...")
             _t3 = _time.time()
             character_count = 0

             for char_name, char_path in character_dirs:
                 skeletons: dict[str, SkeletonData] = {}

                 if char_name in char_skeleton_map:
                     for skeleton_info in char_skeleton_map[char_name]:
                         sk_name = skeleton_info.skeleton_name
                         if (char_name, sk_name) in skeleton_results:
                             skeletons[sk_name] = skeleton_results[(char_name, sk_name)]

                 char_data = CharacterData(
                     path=char_path,
                     skeletons=skeletons
                 )
                 self.character_found.emit(char_name, char_data)
                 character_count += 1

             lprint(f"[扫描] 第四步完成：发送 {character_count} 个角色数据，耗时 {_time.time() - _t3:.2f}s")
             lprint(f"[扫描] 全部完成：{character_count} 个角色，总耗时 {_time.time() - _t_total:.2f}s")
             self.finished.emit(character_count)

         except Exception as e:
             import traceback

             print(f"扫描异常: {str(e)}")
             print(traceback.format_exc())
             self.finished.emit(0)


 class LogFileCheckWorker(QThread):  # → 调用 LogFileCheckWorker()
     """后台检查日志文件存在性的工作线程"""

     progress = Signal(int, int)  # current, total
     log_file_checked = Signal(object)  # anim_data
     finished = Signal()  # 检查完成

     def __init__(self, anim_data_list: List[AnimData]):
         """
         初始化日志文件检查线程

         Args:
             anim_data_list: 需要检查的动画数据列表
         """
         super().__init__()
         self.anim_data_list = anim_data_list

     def run(self):
         """在后台线程中检查日志文件存在性"""
         try:
             total = len(self.anim_data_list)
             for idx, anim_data in enumerate(self.anim_data_list):
                 # 检查三个日志文件的存在性
                 export_fbx_log_path = getattr(anim_data, 'export_fbx_log_path', '')
                 preview_log_path = getattr(anim_data, 'preview_log_path', '')
                 upload_muse_log_path = getattr(anim_data, 'upload_muse_log_path', '')

                 export_fbx_log_exists = os.path.exists(export_fbx_log_path) if export_fbx_log_path else False
                 preview_log_exists = os.path.exists(preview_log_path) if preview_log_path else False
                 upload_muse_log_exists = os.path.exists(upload_muse_log_path) if upload_muse_log_path else False

                 # 更新AnimData的日志文件存在性字段
                 object.__setattr__(anim_data, 'export_fbx_log_exists', export_fbx_log_exists)
                 object.__setattr__(anim_data, 'preview_log_exists', preview_log_exists)
                 object.__setattr__(anim_data, 'upload_muse_log_exists', upload_muse_log_exists)

                 # 发送信号通知UI更新
                 self.log_file_checked.emit(anim_data)

                 # 更新进度
                 self.progress.emit(idx + 1, total)

             self.finished.emit()
         except Exception as e:
             import traceback
             lprint(f"检查日志文件存在性异常: {str(e)}")
             traceback.print_exc()
             self.finished.emit()


 class ExportWorker(QThread):  # → 调用 ExportWorker()
     """导出工作线程"""

     progress = Signal(int, int)  # current, total
     log = Signal(str)
     finished = Signal(bool, str)  # success, message

     def __init__(self, skeletons, engine_root, export_root, config):
         super().__init__()
         self.skeletons = skeletons
         self.engine_root = engine_root
         self.export_root = export_root
         self.config = config

     def run(self):
         try:
             lprint.emit("=" * 60)
             lprint.emit("开始导出动画")
             lprint.emit("=" * 60)
             lprint.emit(f"骨骼数量: {len(self.skeletons)}")
             lprint.emit(f"引擎目录: {self.engine_root}")
             lprint.emit(f"导出目录: {self.export_root}")
             lprint.emit("")

             success_count = 0
             failed_count = 0

             for idx, sk_name in enumerate(self.skeletons):
                 self.progress.emit(idx + 1, len(self.skeletons))
                 lprint.emit(f"[{idx + 1}/{len(self.skeletons)}] 处理骨骼: {sk_name}")

                 try:
                     # 获取ModelLib目录设置
                     modellib_dir = self.ui.modellibDirEdit.text().strip()
                     assert modellib_dir, "ModelLib目录不能为空，请在设置页面配置ModelLib目录路径"
                     assert os.path.exists(modellib_dir), f"ModelLib目录不存在: {modellib_dir}，请在设置页面检查路径配置"

                     args_data = {
                         "engine_root": self.engine_root,
                         "export_root": self.export_root,
                         "modellib_dir": modellib_dir,
                         "timeout_seconds": self.config["timeout_seconds"],
                         "anim_parallel": self.config["anim_parallel"],
                         "anim_max_workers": self.config["anim_max_workers"],
                         "models": self.config.get("models", ""),
                     }

                     atf = anim_to_fbx.AnimToFbx(args_data)
                     result = atf.export_from_sk(sk_name)

                     if result is not None:
                         success_count += 1
                         lprint.emit(f"  ✓ 骨骼 {sk_name} 导出成功")
                     else:
                         failed_count += 1
                         lprint.emit(f"  ✗ 骨骼 {sk_name} 导出失败")

                 except Exception as e:
                     failed_count += 1
                     lprint.emit(f"  ✗ 骨骼 {sk_name} 异常: {str(e)}")

             lprint.emit("")
             lprint.emit("=" * 60)
             lprint.emit("导出完成")
             lprint.emit("=" * 60)
             lprint.emit(f"总骨骼数: {len(self.skeletons)}")
             lprint.emit(f"成功: {success_count}")
             lprint.emit(f"失败: {failed_count}")
             lprint.emit("")

             self.finished.emit(
                 True, f"导出完成！成功: {success_count}, 失败: {failed_count}"
             )

         except Exception as e:
             lprint.emit(f"导出异常: {str(e)}")
             import traceback

             lprint.emit(traceback.format_exc())
             self.finished.emit(False, f"导出失败: {str(e)}")


 class AnimListLoader(QThread):  # → 调用 AnimListLoader()
     """异步加载动画列表的工作线程"""

     progress = Signal(int, int, str)  # current, total, message
     skeleton_loaded = Signal(
         str, dict, int, int
     )  # sk_name, anim_data, exported_count, total_count
     finished = Signal()

     def __init__(
         self, checked_skeletons, skeleton_data, export_root, start_idx, end_idx
     ):
         super().__init__()
         self.checked_skeletons = checked_skeletons
         self.skeleton_data = skeleton_data
         self.export_root = export_root
         self.start_idx = start_idx
         self.end_idx = end_idx

     def run(self):
         try:
             page_skeletons = self.checked_skeletons[self.start_idx : self.end_idx]

             for idx, sk_name in enumerate(page_skeletons):
                 sk_data = self.skeleton_data.get(sk_name)

                 if sk_data:
                     # 统计该骨骼的动画导出情况
                     anim_list = []
                     exported_count = 0
                     total_count = len(sk_data["anims"])

                     for anim_info in sk_data["anims"]:
                         anim_name = anim_info["name"]
                         anim_path = anim_info["path"]
                         fbx_path = os.path.join(
                             self.export_root,
                             "Char",
                             sk_name,
                             "anims",
                             f"{anim_name}.fbx",
                         )
                         is_exported = os.path.exists(fbx_path)

                         if is_exported:
                             exported_count += 1

                         anim_list.append(
                             {
                                 "name": anim_name,
                                 "path": anim_path,
                                 "exported": is_exported,
                             }
                         )

                     # 发送骨骼数据
                     self.skeleton_loaded.emit(
                         sk_name,
                         {"path": sk_data["path"], "anims": anim_list},
                         exported_count,
                         total_count,
                     )

                 # 更新进度
                 self.progress.emit(idx + 1, len(page_skeletons), f"正在加载: {sk_name}")

             self.finished.emit()

         except Exception as e:
             import traceback

             print(f"加载动画列表异常: {str(e)}")
             print(traceback.format_exc())
             self.finished.emit()


 class NoWheelEventFilter(QObject):  # → 调用 NoWheelEventFilter()
     """事件过滤器：禁止滚轮事件"""

     def eventFilter(self, obj, event):
         if event.type() == QEvent.Wheel:
             return True  # 过滤掉滚轮事件
         return super().eventFilter(obj, event)


 def performance_monitor(func):
     """性能分析装饰器，自动记录函数调用和耗时"""
     def wrapper(self, *args, **kwargs):
         if not hasattr(self, '_performance_enabled') or not self._performance_enabled:
             return func(self, *args, **kwargs)  # → 调用 load_anim_page()

         func_name = f"{self.__class__.__name__}.{func.__name__}"
         start_time = time.time()

         try:
             result = func(self, *args, **kwargs)
             duration = time.time() - start_time

             # 记录性能数据
             if hasattr(self, '_record_performance'):
                 self._record_performance(func_name, duration)

             return result
         except Exception as e:
             duration = time.time() - start_time
             if hasattr(self, '_record_performance'):
                 self._record_performance(f"{func_name} [异常]", duration)
             raise

     return wrapper


 class AnimExportUI(QObject):  # → 调用 AnimExportUI()
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
         # 加载 UI 文件

         if not os.path.exists(ui_file_path):
             raise FileNotFoundError(f"UI file not found: {ui_file_path}")

         ui_file = QFile(ui_file_path)
         if not ui_file.open(QFile.ReadOnly):
             raise IOError(f"Cannot open UI file: {ui_file_path}")

         ui_file.close()

         if self.window is None:

                 loader.errorString()

             raise RuntimeError(f"Failed to load UI file: {error_string}")

         # 设置窗口（window 已经是 QMainWindow）

         self.window.installEventFilter(self)

         # 设置窗口图标
         icon_path = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "icon.svg")
         if os.path.exists(icon_path):
             from PySide6.QtGui import QIcon

 # -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
 import os
 import sys

 import argparse
 from anim_upload_muse_tool.messiah_aciton_to_muse import utils

 BLACK_LIST = [
     'heiguafu_old',
 ]

 class AnimToFbx(object):
     def __init__(self, args_data):
         self.engine_root = args_data.get('engine_root')
         self.export_root = args_data.get('export_root')
         self.modellib_dir = args_data.get('modellib_dir')
         self.timeout_seconds = args_data.get('timeout_seconds', 360)  # 每个动画超时时间，默认 6 分钟
         self.anim_parallel = args_data.get('anim_parallel', False)  # 是否启用动画级别多进程
         self.anim_max_workers = args_data.get('anim_max_workers', 8)  # 动画级别最大并行数
         self.models = args_data.get('models', '')  # 直接传入的模型列表（逗号分隔）
         self.batch_size = args_data.get('batch_size', 1)  # 每个 modellib 命令导出的动画数量
         self.get_model_config()

     # noinspection PyUnresolvedReferences
     def get_model_config(self):
         model_config_path = os.path.join(self.engine_root,  # 💡 get_model_config=<function AnimToFbx.get_model_config at 0x00000295174D2CA0> (function)
             'Data/pydataclient/exceldata')  # ⬅️ (第38行) None

         model_config_file = os.path.join(model_config_path, 'model_config.py')
         if os.path.exists(model_config_file):
             sys.path.insert(0,model_config_path)
             import model_config
             self.model_data = model_config.data
         else:
             from anim_upload_muse_tool import model_config
             self.model_data = getattr(model_config, 'data', {})

     def export_from_sk(self,sk_name,anims=None):

         chr_dirs = os.path.join(self.engine_root,'Package/Char',sk_name)

         skeletons = utils.get_skeleton(chr_dirs)
         if not skeletons:
             print('no skeleton:{}'.format(sk_name))
             return

         skeleton_file = skeletons[-1]
         if utils.check_biped(skeleton_file):
             print('skeleton no biped:{}'.format(skeleton_file))
             return

         # 优先使用直接传入的 models 参数
         if self.models:
             model_list = [m.strip() for m in self.models.split(',') if m.strip()]
             print('model_list (from models param):{}'.format(model_list))
         else:
             model_list = utils.get_model_list(self.model_data, skeletons)
             print('model_list (from model_data):{}'.format(model_list))

         # 如果没有 model_list，继续执行但不导出蒙皮
         if not model_list:
             print('no model list, will export animations without skin for:{}'.format(sk_name))
             model_list = []
         if not anims:
             anims = utils.get_anims(chr_dirs)

         export_dir = os.path.join(self.export_root,'Char',sk_name, 'anims')

         # 根据配置选择批量模式或单个动画模式
         if self.anim_parallel:
             # 动画级别多进程：每个命令导出 batch_size 个动画
             cmds = utils.build_export_cmds_per_anim(skeleton_file, model_list, anims, export_dir, batch_size=self.batch_size, modellib_dir=self.modellib_dir)
             utils.batch_run_cmds_parallel(cmds, timeout_seconds=self.timeout_seconds, max_workers=self.anim_max_workers)
         else:
             # 批量模式：多个动画打包成一个命令
             cmds = utils.build_export_cmds(skeleton_file, model_list, anims, export_dir, modellib_dir=self.modellib_dir)
             utils.batch_run_cmds(cmds, timeout_seconds=self.timeout_seconds)

 class AnimData:
     """动画数据 - 统一的数据结构，用于UI显示、上传、拍屏、导出等所有操作"""
     path: str  # 动画文件路径
     res: str   # res字段（用于Muse标签）
     name: str  # 动画名称
     skeleton_name: str = ""  # 骨骼名称  # 💡 skeleton_name='' (str)
     character_name: str = ""  # 角色名称  # 💡 character_name='' (str)
     skeleton_path: str = ""  # 骨骼文件路径

     # 状态字段（由数据中心统一管理）  # 💡 skeleton_path='' (str)
     fbx_path: str = ""  # FBX文件路径（导出后设置）  # 💡 fbx_path='' (str)
     fbx_ske_mesh_ani_path: str = ""  # fbx骨骼网格体动画文件路径  # 💡 fbx_ske_mesh_ani_path='' (str)
     mp4_path: str = ""  # MP4预览文件路径（拍屏后设置）  # 💡 mp4_path='' (str)
     gif_path: str = ""  # GIF预览文件路径（拍屏后设置）

     # 状态标志（由数据中心根据文件存在性自动更新）  # 💡 gif_path='' (str)
     is_exported: bool = False  # 是否已导出FBX  # 💡 is_exported=False (bool)
     is_previewed: bool = False  # 是否已拍屏（MP4和GIF都存在）  # 💡 is_previewed=False (bool)
     is_uploaded: bool = False  # 是否已上传到Muse  # 💡 is_uploaded=False (bool)
     muse_status: str = "未检查"  # Muse状态：未检查/已上传/未上传  # 💡 muse_status='未检查' (str)

     description: str = ""  # Muse简介（从JSON文件读取）

     @property

     @property
     def anim_id(self) -> str:
         """动画ID（自动生成）

         Returns:
             str: 动画ID，格式：char_{角色名}_ske_{骨骼名}_ani_{动画名}
         """
         if not self.character_name or not self.skeleton_name or not self.name:
             return ""
         safe_anim_name = self.name.replace("/", "_").replace("\\", "_").replace(":", "_")
         return f"char_{self.character_name}_ske_{self.skeleton_name}_ani_{safe_anim_name}"

     @property
     def export_fbx_bat_file(self) -> str:

         Returns:
             str: 批处理文件完整路径，格式：{temp_dir}/batch_fbx_export/batch_export_{anim_id}.bat
         """
         anim_id = self.anim_id
         if not anim_id:
             return ""
         import os
         temp_dir = os.environ.get("TEMP", os.environ.get("TMP", ""))
         if not temp_dir:
             return ""
         prefix = "batch_fbx_export"
         bat_filename = f"batch_export_{anim_id}.bat"
         return os.path.join(temp_dir, "H72Messiah_AL_temp", prefix, bat_filename)

     def _initialize_muse_tags(self, tags: List[str]):
         """初始化 muse_tags（仅在未初始化或为空时允许调用）

         Args:
             tags: 标签列表，根据后缀名自动识别：
                  - .anim 结尾：动画路径（res字段）
                  - .skeleton 结尾：骨骼路径
                  - 无后缀名：动画名称
                  最终格式：[动画名, res字段, 骨骼相对路径]
         """
         if self._muse_tags:
             raise AttributeError("muse_tags 已经初始化，不能再次修改")

         # 格式化标签：顺序为 [动画名称, res字段, 骨骼相对路径]，不带前缀
         formatted_tags = []

         # 根据后缀名识别标签类型
         anim_name = None
         res_tag = None
         skeleton_path = None

         for tag in tags:
             if not tag:
                 continue

             tag_normalized = tag.replace("\\", "/")

             # 判断类型：根据后缀名
             if tag_normalized.endswith('.skeleton'):
                 # 骨骼路径
                 skeleton_path = tag_normalized
             elif tag_normalized.endswith('.anim'):
                 # 动画路径（res字段）
                 res_tag = tag_normalized
             else:
                 # 无后缀名，判断为动画名称
                 anim_name = tag

         # 如果未找到，使用self中的值作为后备
         if not anim_name:
             anim_name = self.name

         if not res_tag and self.res:
             res_tag = self.res
             if not res_tag.endswith('.anim'):
                 res_tag = res_tag + '.anim'

         if not skeleton_path:
             skeleton_path = self.skeleton_path

         # 1. 动画名称（放在第一位）
         if anim_name:
             formatted_tags.append(anim_name)

         # 2. res字段（动画路径，放在第二位）
         if res_tag:
             # 转换为从Char开始的相对路径（动画路径处理）
             res_tag = res_tag.replace("\\", "/")

             # 规则：
             # 1) 若路径中包含 Char/，统一裁剪为从 Char/ 开始
             # 2) 若不包含 Char/，通常是相对路径（相对骨骼/工程结构），直接补 Char/ 前缀
             if not res_tag.startswith("Char/"):
                 char_index = res_tag.find("Char/")
                 if char_index != -1:
                     res_tag = res_tag[char_index:]
                 else:
                     res_tag = res_tag.lstrip("./")
                     res_tag = "Char/{}".format(res_tag)

             formatted_tags.append(res_tag)

         # 3. 骨骼路径（放在第三位）
         if skeleton_path:
             # 转换为从Char开始的相对路径
             skeleton_path = skeleton_path.replace("\\", "/")

             # 规则：
             # 1) 若路径中包含 Char/，统一裁剪为从 Char/ 开始
             # 2) 若不包含 Char/，通常是相对路径（相对骨骼/工程结构），直接补 Char/ 前缀
             if not skeleton_path.startswith("Char/"):
                 char_index = skeleton_path.find("Char/")
                 if char_index != -1:
                     skeleton_path = skeleton_path[char_index:]
                 else:
                     skeleton_path = skeleton_path.lstrip("./")
                     skeleton_path = "Char/{}".format(skeleton_path)

             formatted_tags.append(skeleton_path)

         object.__setattr__(self, '_muse_tags', formatted_tags)

     def update_paths(self, export_root: str):
         """根据导出根目录更新所有文件路径（总是设置，确保数据可靠）

         Args:
             export_root: 导出根目录
         """
         assert self.character_name, "character_name 不能为空"
         assert self.skeleton_name, "skeleton_name 不能为空"
         assert self.name, "name 不能为空"
         assert export_root, "export_root 不能为空"

         # FBX路径（不含蒙皮）
         self.fbx_path = os.path.join(
             export_root, "Char", self.character_name, self.skeleton_name, "anims", f"{self.name}.fbx"
         )

         # FBX路径（含蒙皮）
         self.fbx_ske_mesh_ani_path = os.path.join(
             export_root, "Char", self.character_name, self.skeleton_name, "ske_mesh_anims", f"{self.name}.fbx"
         )

         # 拍屏文件路径
         render_root = os.path.join(
             export_root, "Char", self.character_name, self.skeleton_name, "render"
         )
         self.mp4_path = os.path.join(render_root, f"{self.name}.mp4")
         self.gif_path = os.path.join(render_root, f"{self.name}.gif")

     def update_status(self):
         """根据文件存在性更新状态标志（路径必须已设置）"""
         assert self.fbx_path, "fbx_path 必须已设置，请先调用 update_paths()"
         assert self.mp4_path, "mp4_path 必须已设置，请先调用 update_paths()"
         assert self.gif_path, "gif_path 必须已设置，请先调用 update_paths()"

         fbx_exists = os.path.exists(self.fbx_path)
         mp4_exists = os.path.exists(self.mp4_path)
         gif_exists = os.path.exists(self.gif_path)

         from Lugwit_Module import lprint
         lprint(f"[update_status] {self.name}: fbx_path={self.fbx_path}, exists={fbx_exists}")
         lprint(f"[update_status] {self.name}: mp4_path={self.mp4_path}, exists={mp4_exists}")
         lprint(f"[update_status] {self.name}: gif_path={self.gif_path}, exists={gif_exists}")

         self.is_exported = fbx_exists
         self.is_previewed = mp4_exists and gif_exists

     def to_muse_upload_data(self) -> "MuseUploadData":  # ⬅️ (第313行) None
         """转换为Muse上传数据（路径必须已设置）"""
         assert self.fbx_ske_mesh_ani_path or self.fbx_path, "fbx_ske_mesh_ani_path 或 fbx_path 必须已设置"
         assert self.mp4_path, "mp4_path 必须已设置"
         assert self.gif_path, "gif_path 必须已设置"

         return MuseUploadData(
             anim_data=self,
             fbx_path=self.fbx_ske_mesh_ani_path or self.fbx_path,
             mp4_path=self.mp4_path,
             gif_path=self.gif_path
         )

     def get_total_anims(self) -> int:

 class MuseUploadData:
     """Muse上传数据"""
     anim_data: AnimData  # 动画数据
     fbx_path: str  # FBX文件路径（含蒙皮）
     mp4_path: str  # MP4预览文件路径

     def validate(self) -> bool:
         """验证所有文件是否存在"""
         return (
             os.path.exists(self.fbx_path) and
             os.path.exists(self.mp4_path) and
             os.path.exists(self.gif_path)
         )
       # 💡 validate=<function MuseUploadData.validate at 0x00000295175587C0> (function)
     def get_missing_files(self) -> List[str]:  # ⬅️ (第396行) None
         """获取缺失的文件列表"""
         missing = []
         if not os.path.exists(self.fbx_path):
             missing.append(f"FBX: {self.fbx_path}")
         if not os.path.exists(self.mp4_path):
             missing.append(f"MP4: {self.mp4_path}")
         if not os.path.exists(self.gif_path):
             missing.append(f"GIF: {self.gif_path}")
         return missing

     def wait_for_item(self, timeout=None):
         """
         等待队列中有项目

         Args:
             timeout: 超时时间

         Returns:
             bool: 是否有项目可用
         """
         start_time = time.time()
         while self.empty():
             if timeout and (time.time() - start_time) > timeout:
                 return False
             time.sleep(0.01)
         return True

 #!/usr/bin/env python
 # -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
   # 💡 LOW=1 (int)
 """  # 💡 NORMAL=2 (int)
 线程池管理模块  # 💡 HIGH=3 (int)
 =============  # ⬅️ (第58行) None

 提供高级的线程池管理功能，包括工作线程、任务调度、资源管理等。

 🎯 **主要功能**
 - 智能线程池管理
 - 任务优先级调度
 - 线程生命周期管理
 - 资源监控和统计

 📦 **核心类**
 - ThreadPoolManager: 线程池管理器
 - WorkerThread: 工作线程
 - TaskInfo: 任务信息
 - PoolStats: 池统计信息

 🚀 **使用示例**
 ```python
 # 创建线程池
 pool = ThreadPoolManager(max_workers=4)

 # 提交任务
 future = pool.submit(my_function, arg1, arg2)
 result = future.result()

 # 批量提交任务
 futures = pool.map(process_item, item_list)
 results = [f.result() for f in futures]

 # 关闭线程池
 pool.shutdown()
 ```
 """

 import threading
 import queue
 import time
 import concurrent.futures
 from typing import Any, Callable, List, Optional, Dict, Union
 from dataclasses import dataclass
 from enum import Enum

 # 日志函数
 import Lugwit_Module as LM
 lprint = LM.lprint


 class TaskPriority(Enum):
     """任务优先级"""
     LOW = 1
     NORMAL = 2
     HIGH = 3
     URGENT = 4

 #!/usr/bin/env python
 # -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
   # 💡 IDLE='idle' (str)
 """  # 💡 RUNNING='running' (str)
 线程池管理模块  # 💡 STOPPING='stopping' (str)
 =============  # ⬅️ (第66行) None

 提供高级的线程池管理功能，包括工作线程、任务调度、资源管理等。

 🎯 **主要功能**
 - 智能线程池管理
 - 任务优先级调度
 - 线程生命周期管理
 - 资源监控和统计

 📦 **核心类**
 - ThreadPoolManager: 线程池管理器
 - WorkerThread: 工作线程
 - TaskInfo: 任务信息
 - PoolStats: 池统计信息

 🚀 **使用示例**
 ```python
 # 创建线程池
 pool = ThreadPoolManager(max_workers=4)

 # 提交任务
 future = pool.submit(my_function, arg1, arg2)
 result = future.result()

 # 批量提交任务
 futures = pool.map(process_item, item_list)
 results = [f.result() for f in futures]

 # 关闭线程池
 pool.shutdown()
 ```
 """

 import threading
 import queue
 import time
 import concurrent.futures
 from typing import Any, Callable, List, Optional, Dict, Union
 from dataclasses import dataclass
 from enum import Enum

 # 日志函数
 import Lugwit_Module as LM
 lprint = LM.lprint


 class TaskPriority(Enum):
     """任务优先级"""
     LOW = 1
     NORMAL = 2
     HIGH = 3
     URGENT = 4

 #!/usr/bin/env python
 # -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

 """
 锁机制封装模块
 =============

 提供各种高级锁机制的封装，包括智能锁、读写锁、超时锁等。

 🎯 **主要功能**
 - 智能锁管理
 - 读写锁实现
 - 超时锁机制
 - 死锁检测
 - 锁统计和监控

 📦 **核心类**
 - SmartLock: 智能锁，自动管理锁的获取和释放
 - ReadWriteLock: 读写锁，支持多读单写
 - TimeoutLock: 超时锁，支持超时获取
 - DeadlockDetector: 死锁检测器

 🚀 **使用示例**
 ```python
 # 智能锁
 with SmartLock() as lock:
     # 临界区代码
     shared_resource += 1

 # 读写锁
 rw_lock = ReadWriteLock()
 with rw_lock.read_lock():
     # 读操作
     value = shared_data

 with rw_lock.write_lock():
     # 写操作
     shared_data = new_value

 # 超时锁
 timeout_lock = TimeoutLock(timeout=5.0)
 if timeout_lock.acquire():
     try:
         # 临界区代码
         pass
     finally:
         timeout_lock.release()
 ```
 """

 import threading
 import time
 import weakref
 from typing import Optional, Dict, Set, Any, List
 from contextlib import contextmanager
 from collections import defaultdict

 # 日志函数
 import Lugwit_Module as LM
 lprint = LM.lprint


 class SmartLock:
     """
     智能锁

     提供自动管理的锁机制，支持上下文管理器、重入、统计等功能。
     """
       # 💡 acquire=<function SmartLock.acquire at 0x00000295176B0F40> (function)
     def __init__(self, name: str = None, reentrant: bool = True):
         """
         初始化智能锁

         Args:
             name: 锁名称
             reentrant: 是否支持重入
         """
         self.name = name or f"SmartLock-{id(self)}"
         self.reentrant = reentrant

         if reentrant:
             self._lock = threading.RLock()
         else:
             self._lock = threading.Lock()

         self._stats = {  # 💡 release=<function SmartLock.release at 0x00000295176B0FE0> (function)
             'acquire_count': 0,
             'wait_time_total': 0.0,
             'hold_time_total': 0.0,
             'max_wait_time': 0.0,
             'max_hold_time': 0.0,
             'current_holder': None,
             'acquire_time': None
         }
         self._stats_lock = threading.Lock()

     def acquire(self, blocking: bool = True, timeout: float = -1) -> bool:
         """
         获取锁

         Args:
             blocking: 是否阻塞
             timeout: 超时时间

         Returns:
             bool: 是否成功获取锁
         """
         start_time = time.time()

         try:  # 💡 get_stats=<function SmartLock.get_stats at 0x00000295176B11C0> (function)
             if timeout >= 0:  # ⬅️ (第173行) None
                 success = self._lock.acquire(blocking, timeout)
             else:
                 success = self._lock.acquire(blocking)

             if success:
                 wait_time = time.time() - start_time

                 with self._stats_lock:
                     self._stats['acquire_count'] += 1
                     self._stats['wait_time_total'] += wait_time
                     self._stats['max_wait_time'] = max(self._stats['max_wait_time'], wait_time)
                     self._stats['current_holder'] = threading.current_thread().name
                     self._stats['acquire_time'] = time.time()

             return success

         except Exception as e:
             lprint(f"[智能锁] {self.name} 获取锁异常: {e}")
             return False

     def release(self):
         """释放锁"""
         try:
             with self._stats_lock:
                 if self._stats['acquire_time']:
                     hold_time = time.time() - self._stats['acquire_time']
                     self._stats['hold_time_total'] += hold_time
                     self._stats['max_hold_time'] = max(self._stats['max_hold_time'], hold_time)

                 self._stats['current_holder'] = None
                 self._stats['acquire_time'] = None

             self._lock.release()

         except Exception as e:
             lprint(f"[智能锁] {self.name} 释放锁异常: {e}")

     def __enter__(self):
         """上下文管理器入口"""
         self.acquire()
         return self

     def __exit__(self, exc_type, exc_val, exc_tb):
         """上下文管理器出口"""
         self.release()

     def get_stats(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
         """获取锁统计信息"""
         with self._stats_lock:
             stats = self._stats.copy()

             # 计算平均时间
             if stats['acquire_count'] > 0:
                 stats['avg_wait_time'] = stats['wait_time_total'] / stats['acquire_count']
                 stats['avg_hold_time'] = stats['hold_time_total'] / stats['acquire_count']
             else:
                 stats['avg_wait_time'] = 0.0
                 stats['avg_hold_time'] = 0.0

             return stats

     def is_locked(self) -> bool:
         """检查锁是否被持有"""
         return self._stats['current_holder'] is not None

 def check_dependencies():
     """
     检查库的依赖是否满足

     Returns:
         tuple: (是否完整可用, 缺失的依赖列表)
     """
     missing = []
       # 💡 missing=[] (list)
     if not _DISPATCHER_AVAILABLE:
         missing.append("dispatcher (回调调度器)")
     if not _HELPER_AVAILABLE:
         missing.append("helper (线程安全Helper)")
     if not _SYNC_AVAILABLE:
         missing.append("sync (数据同步工具)")
     if not _POOL_AVAILABLE:
         missing.append("pool (线程池管理)")
     if not _LOCKS_AVAILABLE:
         missing.append("locks (锁机制)")

     return len(missing) == 0, missing  # ⬅️ (第115行) (True, [])

 #!/usr/bin/env python
 # -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
 """
 动画UI Helper模块

 负责动画列表的UI更新，继承 ThreadSafeUIHelper 实现自动线程安全。
 参考 digital_workspace 的 ShotsListManager 设计模式。
 """

 from typing import TYPE_CHECKING, List, Optional, Dict, Any, Union, Tuple
 from PySide6.QtWidgets import QListWidgetItem, QTreeWidgetItem
 from PySide6.QtCore import Qt
 from PySide6.QtGui import QColor, QBrush
 import os

 # 导入线程安全基类
 import sys
 baselibs_path = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "@baselibs")
 if baselibs_path not in sys.path:
     sys.path.insert(0, baselibs_path)
 from thread_safe import ThreadSafeUIHelper

 from anim_upload_muse_tool.messiah_aciton_to_muse.data_structures import CharacterData

 import Lugwit_Module as LM
 lprint = LM.lprint

 if TYPE_CHECKING:
     from anim_upload_muse_tool.auto_update_anim_ui import AnimExportUI
 else:
     AnimExportUI = None


 class AnimUIHelper(ThreadSafeUIHelper):
     """
     动画UI Helper - 负责动画列表的UI更新

     继承 ThreadSafeUIHelper，所有公共方法自动线程安全。
     参考 digital_workspace 的 ShotsListManager 设计模式。

     ⚠️ 重要架构说明：
     本类的所有公共方法（带有 _from_data_center 参数的）只能由数据中心（AnimDataCenter）调用。
     这些方法不应该被直接调用，必须通过数据中心来调用。

     _from_data_center 参数的作用：
     - 这是一个文档性参数，用于明确标识调用来源
     - 数据中心调用时必须传递 _from_data_center=True
     - 不要直接调用这些方法，应该通过数据中心的方法来调用
     - 例如：不要直接调用 helper.update_anim_export_status(...)
           应该通过 data_center.update_anim_export_status(...) 来调用
     """

     def __init__(self, main_window: "AnimExportUI"):
         """
         初始化UI Helper

         Args:
             main_window: 主窗口实例
         """
         super(AnimUIHelper, self).__init__(main_window, debug_mode=False)  # 💡 add_character_to_list=<function AnimUIHelper.add_character_to_list at 0x0000029517635F80> (function)
         self.main_window = main_window
         self.skeleton_list = main_window.ui.skeletonList

     def add_character_to_list(self, char_name: str, char_data: CharacterData, _from_data_center: bool = False) -> None:  # 💡 clear_character_list=<function AnimUIHelper.clear_character_list at 0x00000295176B2C00> (function)
         """
         添加角色到列表（自动线程安全）

         ⚠️ 注意：此方法只能由数据中心（AnimDataCenter）调用，不要直接调用。
         应该通过 data_center 的方法来调用，数据中心会自动传递 _from_data_center=True。

         Args:
             char_name: 角色名称
             char_data: 角色数据
             _from_data_center: 是否来自数据中心调用（数据中心必须传递 True，用于文档说明）
         """

         # 使用数据类的方法获取统计信息
         total_anims = char_data.get_total_anims()
         skeleton_count = char_data.get_skeleton_count()

         # 阻止信号，避免每次添加都触发 UI 更新
         self.skeleton_list.blockSignals(True)

         # 添加到列表（带复选框，默认不勾选）
         item = QListWidgetItem(f"{char_name} ({skeleton_count} 骨骼, {total_anims} 动画)")
         item.setData(Qt.UserRole, char_name)
         item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemIsUserCheckable)
         item.setCheckState(Qt.Unchecked)  # 默认不勾选
         self.skeleton_list.addItem(item)

         # 恢复信号
         self.skeleton_list.blockSignals(False)

     def clear_character_list(self) -> None:
         """清空角色列表（自动线程安全）"""
         self.skeleton_list.clear()  # 💡 update_anim_list=<function AnimUIHelper.update_anim_list at 0x00000295176B2B60> (function)

     def update_anim_list(self, checked_char_names: List[str], _from_data_center: bool = False) -> None:
         """
         更新动画列表显示（自动线程安全）

         ⚠️ 注意：此方法只能由数据中心（AnimDataCenter）调用，不要直接调用。
         应该通过 data_center 的方法来调用，数据中心会自动传递 _from_data_center=True。

         UI辅助器自己检查哪些角色被勾选，然后决定是否更新动画列表。
         不需要数据中心传递勾选列表。

         Args:
             checked_char_names: 勾选的角色名称列表（已废弃，不再使用，由UI辅助器自己检查）
             _from_data_center: 是否来自数据中心调用（数据中心必须传递 True，用于文档说明）
         """

         # UI辅助器自己检查勾选状态，决定是否更新动画列表
         # 检查是否有勾选的角色（skeletonList 中存储的是角色，虽然名字叫 skeletonList）
         if hasattr(self.main_window, 'anim_current_page') and hasattr(self.main_window.ui, 'skeletonList'):
             # 检查是否有勾选的角色
             has_checked = False
             for i in range(self.main_window.ui.skeletonList.count()):
                 item = self.main_window.ui.skeletonList.item(i)
                 if item and item.checkState() == Qt.Checked:
                     char_name = item.data(Qt.UserRole)
                     if char_name:  # 跳过分割线（没有UserRole数据）
                         has_checked = True
                         break
               # 💡 update_statistics=<function AnimUIHelper.update_statistics at 0x00000295176B2CA0> (function)
             # 只有在有勾选的角色时才更新动画列表，避免扫描过程中的无效调用
             if has_checked and hasattr(self.main_window, 'load_anim_page'):
                 self.main_window.load_anim_page()

     def update_statistics(self, stats: Dict[str, int]) -> None:
         """
         更新统计信息显示（自动线程安全）

         Args:
             stats: 统计信息字典，包含 total, exported, previewed, uploaded
         """
         if not hasattr(self.main_window.ui, 'animCountLabel'):
             return

         total = stats.get('total', 0)
         exported = stats.get('exported', 0)
         previewed = stats.get('previewed', 0)
         uploaded = stats.get('uploaded', 0)

         if total > 0:
             export_pct = (exported / total) * 100
             preview_pct = (previewed / total) * 100
             muse_pct = (uploaded / total) * 100
             self.main_window.ui.animCountLabel.setText(
                 f"已导出: {exported}/{total} ({export_pct:.1f}%) | "
                 f"已拍屏: {previewed}/{total} ({preview_pct:.1f}%) | "
                 f"已上传Muse: {uploaded}/{total} ({muse_pct:.1f}%)"
             )
         else:
             self.main_window.ui.animCountLabel.setText(
                 "已导出: 0/0 | 已拍屏: 0/0 | 已上传Muse: 0/0"
             )

     def update_anim_export_status(self, item: Optional[QTreeWidgetItem], status: str, color: Union[QColor, QBrush, Qt.GlobalColor], _from_data_center: bool = False) -> None:
         """
         更新动画项的导出状态（自动线程安全）

         ⚠️ 注意：此方法只能由数据中心（AnimDataCenter）调用，不要直接调用。
         应该通过 data_center.update_anim_export_status(...) 来调用，数据中心会自动传递 _from_data_center=True。

         Args:
             item: QTreeWidgetItem对象
             status: 状态文本（如"已导出"、"导出失败"等）
             color: 颜色对象（Qt颜色常量）  # 💡 update_anim_export_status=<function AnimUIHelper.update_anim_export_status at 0x00000295176B2D40> (function)
             _from_data_center: 是否来自数据中心调用（数据中心必须传递 True，用于文档说明）
         """

         if item is None:
             return

         try:
             item.setText(1, status)
             item.setForeground(1, color)

             # 同时更新数据中心中的动画状态
             anim_data = item.data(0, Qt.UserRole)
             if anim_data and hasattr(anim_data, 'is_exported'):
                 # 更新导出状态
                 if status == "已导出":
                     anim_data.is_exported = True
                     # 更新文件路径状态
                     if hasattr(anim_data, 'update_status'):
                         anim_data.update_status()
                 elif status in ["导出失败", "验证失败"]:
                     anim_data.is_exported = False

             # 保存到AnimData
             if anim_data:
                 # 只保存非"检查中..."的状态
                 if status not in ["检查中...", "处理中...", "导出中..."]:
                     object.__setattr__(anim_data, 'export_status_text', status)
         except RuntimeError:
             # UI对象已被删除，忽略
             pass
         except Exception as e:
             lprint.error(f"更新动画导出状态失败: {str(e)}")

     def update_anim_preview_status(self, item: Optional[QTreeWidgetItem], status: str, color: Union[QColor, QBrush, Qt.GlobalColor], _from_data_center: bool = False) -> None:
         """
         更新动画项的拍屏状态（自动线程安全）

         ⚠️ 注意：此方法只能由数据中心（AnimDataCenter）调用，不要直接调用。
         应该通过 data_center.update_anim_preview_status(...) 来调用，数据中心会自动传递 _from_data_center=True。
           # 💡 update_anim_preview_status=<function AnimUIHelper.update_anim_preview_status at 0x00000295176B2DE0> (function)
         Args:
             item: QTreeWidgetItem对象
             status: 状态文本（如"已拍屏"、"拍屏失败"、"拍屏中..."等）
             color: 颜色对象（Qt颜色常量）
             _from_data_center: 是否来自数据中心调用（数据中心必须传递 True，用于文档说明）
         """

         if item is None:
             return

         try:
             # 拍屏状态应该更新第3列（列索引从0开始：0=动画名，1=导出状态，2=Muse状态，3=拍屏状态）
             anim_data = item.data(0, Qt.UserRole) if item else None
             anim_name = anim_data.name if anim_data and hasattr(anim_data, 'name') else "未知"
             lprint.debug(f"[UI辅助器] 更新拍屏状态UI: {anim_name} -> 第3列: {status}")
             item.setText(3, status)
             item.setForeground(3, color)
             lprint.debug(f"[UI辅助器] 拍屏状态UI更新成功: {anim_name}")

             # 保存到AnimData
             if anim_data:
                 # 保存所有状态，包括处理中状态（如"拍屏中..."、"处理中..."等）
                 object.__setattr__(anim_data, 'preview_status_text', status)
         except RuntimeError:
             # UI对象已被删除，忽略
             anim_data = item.data(0, Qt.UserRole) if item else None
             anim_name = anim_data.name if anim_data and hasattr(anim_data, 'name') else "未知"
             lprint.warning(f"[UI辅助器] UI项已被删除，无法更新拍屏状态: {anim_name}")
         except Exception as e:
             anim_data = item.data(0, Qt.UserRole) if item else None
             anim_name = anim_data.name if anim_data and hasattr(anim_data, 'name') else "未知"
             lprint.error(f"[UI辅助器] 更新动画拍屏状态失败: {anim_name} - {str(e)}")

     def update_anim_muse_status(self, item: Optional[QTreeWidgetItem], is_uploaded: bool, _from_data_center: bool = False) -> None:
         """
         更新动画项的Muse上传状态（自动线程安全）

         ⚠️ 注意：此方法只能由数据中心（AnimDataCenter）调用，不要直接调用。
         应该通过 data_center.update_anim_muse_status(...) 来调用，数据中心会自动传递 _from_data_center=True。

         Args:
             item: QTreeWidgetItem对象
             is_uploaded: 是否已上传到Muse（True=已上传，False=未上传）
             _from_data_center: 是否来自数据中心调用（数据中心必须传递 True，用于文档说明）
         """

         if item is None:  # 💡 update_anim_muse_status=<function AnimUIHelper.update_anim_muse_status at 0x00000295176B2E80> (function)
             return

         try:
             # 获取AnimData对象，检查日志文件状态
             anim_data = item.data(0, Qt.UserRole) if item else None
             upload_muse_log_exists = getattr(anim_data, 'upload_muse_log_exists', False) if anim_data else False

             muse_status_text = None
             if is_uploaded:
                 item.setText(2, "已上传")
                 item.setForeground(2, Qt.green)
                 muse_status_text = "已上传"
             elif upload_muse_log_exists:
                 # 日志文件存在但未上传，说明上传失败
                 item.setText(2, "失败")
                 item.setForeground(2, Qt.red)
                 upload_muse_log_path = getattr(anim_data, 'upload_muse_log_path', '') if anim_data else ''
                 item.setToolTip(2, f"上传失败：日志文件存在但Muse状态为未上传\n日志: {upload_muse_log_path}")
                 muse_status_text = "失败"
             else:
                 item.setText(2, "未上传")
                 item.setForeground(2, Qt.gray)
                 muse_status_text = "未上传"

             # 保存到AnimData
             if muse_status_text and anim_data:
                 object.__setattr__(anim_data, 'muse_status', muse_status_text)
         except RuntimeError:
             # UI对象已被删除，忽略
             pass
         except Exception as e:
             lprint.error(f"更新动画Muse状态失败: {str(e)}")

     def refresh_anim_status_by_data(self, item: Optional[QTreeWidgetItem], _from_data_center: bool = False) -> None:
         """
         根据QTreeWidgetItem刷新动画状态（自动线程安全）

         ⚠️ 注意：此方法只能由数据中心（AnimDataCenter）调用，不要直接调用。
         应该通过 data_center 的方法来调用，数据中心会自动传递 _from_data_center=True。

         从item中获取AnimData，然后更新三列状态（导出、Muse、拍屏）。

         Args:
             item: QTreeWidgetItem对象（包含AnimData）
             _from_data_center: 是否来自数据中心调用（数据中心必须传递 True，用于文档说明）
         """

         if item is None:
             return

         try:
             # 从item中获取AnimData
             anim_data = item.data(0, Qt.UserRole)
             if not anim_data:
                 return
         except RuntimeError:
             # UI对象已被删除，忽略
             return
         except Exception as e:
             lprint.warning(f"获取动画数据失败: {str(e)}")
             return

         try:
             # 更新第1列：导出状态
             fbx_path = getattr(anim_data, 'fbx_path', '')
             fbx_exists = os.path.exists(fbx_path) if fbx_path else False
             export_fbx_log_exists = getattr(anim_data, 'export_fbx_log_exists', False)
             if export_fbx_log_exists and not fbx_exists:
                 # 日志文件存在但FBX文件不存在，说明导出失败
                 item.setText(1, "失败")
                 item.setForeground(1, Qt.red)
                 item.setToolTip(1, f"导出失败：日志文件存在但FBX文件不存在\n日志: {getattr(anim_data, 'export_fbx_log_path', '')}")
             elif fbx_exists:
                 item.setText(1, "已导出")
                 item.setForeground(1, Qt.green)
             else:
                 item.setText(1, "未导出")
                 item.setForeground(1, Qt.gray)

             # 更新第2列：Muse状态
             is_uploaded = getattr(anim_data, 'is_uploaded', False)
             upload_muse_log_exists = getattr(anim_data, 'upload_muse_log_exists', False)
             if upload_muse_log_exists and not is_uploaded:
                 # 日志文件存在但Muse状态为未上传，可能是上传失败
                 item.setText(2, "失败")
                 item.setForeground(2, Qt.red)
                 item.setToolTip(2, f"上传失败：日志文件存在但Muse状态为未上传\n日志: {getattr(anim_data, 'upload_muse_log_path', '')}")
             elif is_uploaded:
                 item.setText(2, "已上传")
                 item.setForeground(2, Qt.green)
             else:
                 item.setText(2, "未检查")
                 item.setForeground(2, Qt.gray)

             # 更新第3列：拍屏状态
             mp4_path = getattr(anim_data, 'mp4_path', '')
             gif_path = getattr(anim_data, 'gif_path', '')  # 💡 refresh_anim_status_by_data=<function AnimUIHelper.refresh_anim_status_by_data at 0x00000295176B2F20> (function)
             fbx_ske_mesh_ani_path = getattr(anim_data, 'fbx_ske_mesh_ani_path', '')
             mp4_exists = os.path.exists(mp4_path) if mp4_path else False
             gif_exists = os.path.exists(gif_path) if gif_path else False
             fbx_ske_mesh_exists = os.path.exists(fbx_ske_mesh_ani_path) if fbx_ske_mesh_ani_path else False
             preview_log_exists = getattr(anim_data, 'preview_log_exists', False)

             if preview_log_exists and not mp4_exists and not gif_exists:
                 # 日志文件存在但拍屏文件都不存在，说明拍屏失败
                 item.setText(3, "失败")
                 item.setForeground(3, Qt.red)
                 item.setToolTip(3, f"拍屏失败：日志文件存在但输出文件不存在\n日志: {getattr(anim_data, 'preview_log_path', '')}")
             elif mp4_exists and gif_exists:
                 item.setText(3, "✓")
                 item.setForeground(3, Qt.green)
             elif mp4_exists or gif_exists:
                 item.setText(3, "部分")
                 item.setForeground(3, Qt.yellow)
             elif not fbx_ske_mesh_exists:
                 # 如果fbx骨骼网格体动画不存在，显示警告
                 item.setText(3, "⚠需蒙皮")
                 item.setForeground(3, Qt.yellow)
                 item.setToolTip(3, "拍屏需要fbx骨骼网格体动画文件，请先导出")
             else:
                 item.setText(3, "✗")
                 item.setForeground(3, Qt.gray)
         except RuntimeError:
             # UI对象已被删除，忽略
             anim_name = getattr(anim_data, 'name', '未知') if anim_data else '未知'
             lprint.warning(f"UI项已被删除，无法更新动画状态: {anim_name}")
         except Exception as e:
             anim_name = getattr(anim_data, 'name', '未知') if anim_data else '未知'
             lprint.warning(f"更新动画状态失败: {anim_name} - {str(e)}")

     def update_skeleton_rows_muse_statistics(self, skeleton_stats: Dict[Tuple[str, str], Tuple[int, int]], _from_data_center: bool = False) -> None:
         """
         更新所有骨骼行的Muse状态统计（自动线程安全）

         ⚠️ 注意：此方法只能由数据中心（AnimDataCenter）调用，不要直接调用。
         应该通过 data_center.on_muse_status_check_complete() 来调用，数据中心会自动传递 _from_data_center=True。

         Args:
             skeleton_stats: 骨骼统计字典，格式为 {(char_name, sk_name): (uploaded_count, total_count)}
             _from_data_center: 是否来自数据中心调用（数据中心必须传递 True，用于文档说明）
         """
         try:
             from PySide6.QtGui import QColor
             light_blue = QColor(100, 200, 255)  # 亮蓝色

             # 遍历所有角色节点  # 💡 update_skeleton_rows_muse_statistics=<function AnimUIHelper.update_skeleton_rows_muse_statistics at 0x00000295176B2FC0> (function)
             for i in range(self.main_window.ui.animTree.topLevelItemCount()):  # ⬅️ (第436行) '<cell at 0x00000295176631C0: empty>'
                 char_item = self.main_window.ui.animTree.topLevelItem(i)
                 if not char_item:
                     continue

                 char_name = char_item.text(0)

                 # 遍历该角色下的所有骨骼节点
                 for j in range(char_item.childCount()):
                     sk_item = char_item.child(j)
                     if not sk_item:
                         continue

                     # 提取骨骼名称（去除统计信息）
                     sk_text = sk_item.text(0)
                     if '(' in sk_text:
                         sk_name = sk_text.split('(')[0].strip()
                     else:
                         sk_name = sk_text.strip()

                     # 从统计字典中获取该骨骼的统计信息
                     key = (char_name, sk_name)
                     if key in skeleton_stats:
                         uploaded_count, total_count = skeleton_stats[key]
                         # 更新骨骼行的第2列（Muse状态列）统计
                         sk_item.setText(2, f"{uploaded_count}/{total_count}")
                         sk_item.setForeground(2, light_blue)
                         lprint.debug(f"[UI辅助器] 更新骨骼行统计: {char_name}/{sk_name} - Muse状态: {uploaded_count}/{total_count}")
         except Exception as e:
             lprint.warning(f"更新骨骼行Muse状态统计失败: {str(e)}")
             import traceback
             traceback.print_exc()

     def update_anim_count_label(self, total: int, exported: int, previewed: int, muse: int, _from_data_center: bool = False) -> None:
         """
         更新动画数量标签（自动线程安全）

         ⚠️ 注意：此方法只能由数据中心（AnimDataCenter）调用，不要直接调用。
         应该通过 data_center.update_anim_count_label() 来调用，数据中心会自动传递 _from_data_center=True。

         Args:
             total: 总动画数
             exported: 已导出数量
             previewed: 已拍屏数量
             muse: 已上传Muse数量
             _from_data_center: 是否来自数据中心调用（数据中心必须传递 True，用于文档说明）
         """
         try:
             if total > 0:
                 export_pct = (exported / total) * 100
                 preview_pct = (previewed / total) * 100
                 muse_pct = (muse / total) * 100
                 text = (
                     f"已导出: {exported}/{total} ({export_pct:.1f}%) | "
                     f"已拍屏: {previewed}/{total} ({preview_pct:.1f}%) | "
                     f"已上传Muse: {muse}/{total} ({muse_pct:.1f}%)"
                 )
             else:
                 text = "已导出: 0/0 | 已拍屏: 0/0 | 已上传Muse: 0/0"

             self.main_window.ui.animCountLabel.setText(text)
             lprint.debug(f"[UI辅助器] 更新动画数量标签: {text}")
         except Exception as e:
             lprint.warning(f"更新动画数量标签失败: {str(e)}")
             import traceback
             traceback.print_exc()

 def detect_file_encoding(file_path: str) -> str:
     """
     检测文件的编码

     Args:
         file_path: 文件路径

     Returns:
         检测到的编码名称（如'utf-8', 'gbk'等），默认返回'utf-8'
           # 💡 sizeHint=<function LineNumberArea.sizeHint at 0x000002951778BC40> (function)
     Raises:  # ⬅️ (第95行) '<cell at 0x0000029517722380: empty>'
         FileNotFoundError: 文件不存在
         IOError: 文件读取失败
     """
     if not os.path.exists(file_path):
         raise FileNotFoundError(f"文件不存在: {file_path}")

     try:
         with open(file_path, 'rb') as f:
             content_bytes = f.read()
         return detect_encoding(content_bytes)
     except IOError as e:
         raise IOError(f"读取文件失败: {file_path}, 错误: {str(e)}")

     def highlight_current_line(self):
         """高亮当前行（只读模式下不高亮）"""
         from PySide6.QtWidgets import QTextEdit

         extra_selections = []

         # 只读模式下也可以高亮，用于显示当前浏览的行
         if True:  # 总是高亮当前行，方便阅读
             selection = QTextEdit.ExtraSelection()

             line_color = QColor(64, 64, 64)  # 深灰色

             selection.format.setBackground(line_color)
             selection.format.setProperty(QTextFormat.FullWidthSelection, True)
             selection.cursor = self.textCursor()
             selection.cursor.clearSelection()
             extra_selections.append(selection)

         self.setExtraSelections(extra_selections)

 # -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
 """
 Muse标签和简介更新进度对话框模块
 """

 from PySide6.QtWidgets import (
     QDialog,
     QVBoxLayout,
     QHBoxLayout,
     QLabel,
     QProgressBar,
     QTextEdit,
     QDialogButtonBox,
     QApplication,
 )
 from PySide6.QtCore import Qt


 class MuseUpdateProgressDialog(QDialog):
     """Muse标签和简介更新进度对话框"""

     def __init__(self, parent, total_count: int = 1, anim_name: str = "", title: str = None, title_text: str = None, max_concurrent: int = None):
         """
         Args:
             parent: 父窗口
             total_count: 总数量（单个更新时为1，批量更新时为动画数量）
             anim_name: 当前更新的动画名称（单个更新时使用）
             title: 窗口标题（可选，默认根据is_single自动设置）
             title_text: 标题标签文本（可选，默认根据is_single自动设置）
             max_concurrent: 最大并发线程数（可选，用于显示线程信息）
         """
         super().__init__(parent)
         self.total_count = total_count
         self.current_index = 0
         self.success_count = 0
         self.fail_count = 0
         self.skip_count = 0
         self.verify_fail_count = 0
         self.is_single = (total_count == 1)
         self.max_concurrent = max_concurrent
         self.running_tasks = set()  # 当前运行中的任务集合（anim_name）
         self.completed_tasks = set()  # 已完成的任务集合（anim_name）
         if title is None:
             title = "更新Muse标签和简介" if self.is_single else "批量更新Muse标签和简介"
         self.setWindowTitle(title)
         if title_text is None:
             title_text = None  # 将在_setup_ui中根据is_single设置
         self.title_text = title_text
         self.setMinimumWidth(600)
         self.setMinimumHeight(400 if not self.is_single else 300)
         self._setup_ui(anim_name)

     def _setup_ui(self, anim_name: str):
         """初始化UI"""
         layout = QVBoxLayout(self)

         # 标题标签
         if self.title_text is not None:
             # 使用自定义标题文本
             title_label_text = self.title_text
         elif self.is_single:
             title_label_text = f"正在更新: {anim_name}"
         else:
             title_label_text = f"正在批量更新 {self.total_count} 个动画的标签和简介"
         self.title_label = QLabel(title_label_text)
         self.title_label.setStyleSheet("font-weight: bold; font-size: 12pt;")
         layout.addWidget(self.title_label)

         # 进度条
         self.progress_bar = QProgressBar()
         self.progress_bar.setMaximum(self.total_count)
         self.progress_bar.setValue(0)
         layout.addWidget(self.progress_bar)

         # 状态文本
         self.status_label = QLabel("准备中...")
         layout.addWidget(self.status_label)

         # 详细日志（批量更新时显示）
         if not self.is_single:
             self.log_text = QTextEdit()
             self.log_text.setReadOnly(True)
             self.log_text.setMaximumHeight(250)
             layout.addWidget(self.log_text)

         # 线程和任务信息（批量模式时显示）
         if not self.is_single:
             info_layout = QHBoxLayout()
             if self.max_concurrent is not None:
                 self.thread_info_label = QLabel(f"并发线程数: {self.max_concurrent} | 总任务数: {self.total_count}")
             else:
                 self.thread_info_label = QLabel(f"总任务数: {self.total_count}")
             self.thread_info_label.setStyleSheet("color: #888888; font-size: 9pt;")
             info_layout.addWidget(self.thread_info_label)
             info_layout.addStretch()
             layout.addLayout(info_layout)

         # 统计信息
         stats_layout = QHBoxLayout()
         self.stats_label = QLabel("成功: 0 | 失败: 0 | 跳过: 0 | 验证失败: 0")
         stats_layout.addWidget(self.stats_label)
         stats_layout.addStretch()
         layout.addLayout(stats_layout)

         # 按钮（完成后显示）
         self.button_box = QDialogButtonBox(QDialogButtonBox.Ok)
         self.button_box.button(QDialogButtonBox.Ok).setText("关闭")
         self.button_box.setVisible(False)
         self.button_box.accepted.connect(self.accept)
         layout.addWidget(self.button_box)

     def update_progress(self, current_index: int, anim_name: str, status: str, is_success: bool = None, error_msg: str = ""):
         """
         更新进度

         Args:
             current_index: 当前索引（从1开始）
             anim_name: 动画名称
             status: 状态文本
             is_success: 是否成功（None=进行中，True=成功，False=失败）
             error_msg: 错误消息（失败时）
         """
         self.current_index = current_index
         self.progress_bar.setValue(current_index)

         # 更新运行中的任务数（根据状态判断）
         if is_success is None:
             # 进行中：添加到运行中集合
             if anim_name not in self.completed_tasks:
                 self.running_tasks.add(anim_name)
         elif is_success is not None:
             # 已完成（成功或失败）：从运行中移除，添加到已完成
             self.running_tasks.discard(anim_name)
             self.completed_tasks.add(anim_name)

         if self.is_single:
             self.status_label.setText(status)
         else:
             # 更新标题（如果使用自定义标题文本，则根据自定义格式更新）
             if self.title_text is not None and "上传" in self.title_text:
                 # 上传模式：显示"正在上传 (X/总数): 动画名"
                 self.title_label.setText(f"正在上传 ({current_index}/{self.total_count}): {anim_name}")
             else:
                 # 更新标签模式：显示"正在更新 (X/总数): 动画名"
                 self.title_label.setText(f"正在更新 ({current_index}/{self.total_count}): {anim_name}")
             self.status_label.setText(status)

             # 更新线程和任务信息
             if hasattr(self, 'thread_info_label'):
                 running_count = len(self.running_tasks)
                 completed_count = len(self.completed_tasks)
                 waiting_count = max(0, self.total_count - current_index)
                 if self.max_concurrent is not None:
                     info_text = f"并发线程数: {self.max_concurrent} | 总任务数: {self.total_count} | 运行中: {running_count} | 已完成: {completed_count} | 等待中: {waiting_count}"
                 else:
                     info_text = f"总任务数: {self.total_count} | 运行中: {running_count} | 已完成: {completed_count} | 等待中: {waiting_count}"
                 self.thread_info_label.setText(info_text)

             # 添加日志
             status_icon = "✓" if is_success is True else "✗" if is_success is False else "→"  # 💡 update_progress=<function MuseUpdateProgressDialog.update_progress at 0x000002951782A8E0> (function)
             log_line = f"[{current_index}/{self.total_count}] {status_icon} {anim_name}: {status}"
             if error_msg:
                 log_line += f" ({error_msg})"
             self.log_text.append(log_line)
             # 自动滚动到底部
             self.log_text.verticalScrollBar().setValue(self.log_text.verticalScrollBar().maximum())

         # 更新统计
         if is_success is True:
             self.success_count += 1
         elif is_success is False:
             self.fail_count += 1

         self._update_stats()

         # 处理事件，确保UI更新
         QApplication.processEvents()

     def add_skip(self, anim_name: str, reason: str = "Muse状态为'未上传'"):
         """添加跳过记录"""
         self.skip_count += 1
         # 跳过也算作已完成  # 💡 add_skip=<function MuseUpdateProgressDialog.add_skip at 0x000002951782A980> (function)
         self.running_tasks.discard(anim_name)
         self.completed_tasks.add(anim_name)
         if not self.is_single:
             self.log_text.append(f"⏭ {anim_name}: 已跳过（{reason}）")
             self.log_text.verticalScrollBar().setValue(self.log_text.verticalScrollBar().maximum())
             # 更新线程和任务信息
             if hasattr(self, 'thread_info_label'):
                 running_count = len(self.running_tasks)
                 completed_count = len(self.completed_tasks)
                 waiting_count = max(0, self.total_count - self.current_index)
                 if self.max_concurrent is not None:
                     info_text = f"并发线程数: {self.max_concurrent} | 总任务数: {self.total_count} | 运行中: {running_count} | 已完成: {completed_count} | 等待中: {waiting_count}"
                 else:
                     info_text = f"总任务数: {self.total_count} | 运行中: {running_count} | 已完成: {completed_count} | 等待中: {waiting_count}"
                 self.thread_info_label.setText(info_text)
         self._update_stats()
         QApplication.processEvents()

     def add_verify_fail(self, anim_name: str):
         """添加验证失败记录"""
         self.verify_fail_count += 1
         # 验证失败也算作已完成  # 💡 add_verify_fail=<function MuseUpdateProgressDialog.add_verify_fail at 0x000002951782AA20> (function)
         self.running_tasks.discard(anim_name)
         self.completed_tasks.add(anim_name)
         if not self.is_single:
             self.log_text.append(f"⚠ {anim_name}: 验证失败（标签或简介不一致）")
             self.log_text.verticalScrollBar().setValue(self.log_text.verticalScrollBar().maximum())
             # 更新线程和任务信息
             if hasattr(self, 'thread_info_label'):
                 running_count = len(self.running_tasks)  # ⬅️ (第230行) '<cell at 0x0000029517721E10: empty>'
                 completed_count = len(self.completed_tasks)
                 waiting_count = max(0, self.total_count - self.current_index)
                 if self.max_concurrent is not None:
                     info_text = f"并发线程数: {self.max_concurrent} | 总任务数: {self.total_count} | 运行中: {running_count} | 已完成: {completed_count} | 等待中: {waiting_count}"
                 else:
                     info_text = f"总任务数: {self.total_count} | 运行中: {running_count} | 已完成: {completed_count} | 等待中: {waiting_count}"
                 self.thread_info_label.setText(info_text)
         self._update_stats()
         QApplication.processEvents()

     def _update_stats(self):
         """更新统计信息"""
         stats_text = f"成功: {self.success_count} | 失败: {self.fail_count} | 跳过: {self.skip_count}"
         if self.verify_fail_count > 0:
             stats_text += f" | 验证失败: {self.verify_fail_count}"
         self.stats_label.setText(stats_text)

     def finish(self, final_status: str = ""):
         """完成更新"""
         self.progress_bar.setValue(self.total_count)

         if final_status:
             self.status_label.setText(final_status)

         # 显示完成消息
         if self.is_single:
             if self.success_count > 0:
                 self.status_label.setText("✓ 更新成功")
                 self.status_label.setStyleSheet("color: green; font-weight: bold;")
             else:
                 self.status_label.setText("✗ 更新失败")
                 self.status_label.setStyleSheet("color: red; font-weight: bold;")
         else:
             summary = f"更新完成！成功: {self.success_count}, 失败: {self.fail_count}, 跳过: {self.skip_count}"
             if self.verify_fail_count > 0:
                 summary += f", 验证失败: {self.verify_fail_count}"
             self.status_label.setText(summary)
             self.log_text.append("")
             self.log_text.append("=" * 60)
             self.log_text.append(summary)

         # 显示关闭按钮
         self.button_box.setVisible(True)
         QApplication.processEvents()

 # Python 2/3 兼容性处理
 if sys.version_info[0] >= 3:
     string_types = str
     integer_types = int
 else:
     string_types = basestring
     integer_types = (int, long)


 class CredentialUtil(object):
     @staticmethod
     def encode(data):
         if sys.version_info[0] >= 3:
             data = data.encode('utf-8')
         return base64.b64encode(data)

     @staticmethod
     def decode(data):
         result = base64.b64decode(data)
         if sys.version_info[0] >= 3:
             return result.decode('utf-8')
         return result

 def _from_byte_list(byte_list):
     """从字节列表创建字节串"""
     if sys.version_info[0] >= 3:
         return bytes(byte_list)
     else:
         return ''.join(chr(b) for b in byte_list)

 # -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

 import os
 import time
 import base64
 import datetime
 import logging

 try:
     from urllib.parse import urlencode
 except ImportError:
     from urllib import urlencode

 import certifi
 import requests
 import tusclient.client

 from muse_python_api.exceptions import MuseError, MuseTokenError
 from muse_python_api.utils import CredentialUtil, encrypt_email
 from muse_python_api.interface import MuseInterface
 from muse_python_api.config import CLIENT_NAME_MAP
 import sys
 sys.path.append(r"D:\TD_Depot\Software\Lugwit_syncPlug\lugwit_insapp\trayapp\Lib")
 import Lugwit_Module as LM
 lprint = LM.lprint
 logger = logging.getLogger('Muse Pipe Debug Info')


 class _MuseBase(object):
     def __init__(self, email, name='wuzu'):
         self.email = email
         self._verify = certifi.where() if os.path.exists(certifi.where()) else False

         if os.environ.get('MUSE_DEV', '0') == '1':
             client_name = CLIENT_NAME_MAP['dev']['name']
             self._client_info = CLIENT_NAME_MAP['dev']['client']
         else:
             client_name = CLIENT_NAME_MAP[name]['name']
             self._client_info = CLIENT_NAME_MAP[name]['client']

         self._email = encrypt_email(self.email, client_name)
         self._token = None
         self._token_expired_at = None

     def _get_token(self):
         try:
             encrypted_credentials = base64.b64encode(
                 CredentialUtil.encode('{}:{}'.format(
                     self._client_info.client_id,
                     self._client_info.client_secret)
                 ))
             headers = {
                 'Authorization': 'Basic {}'.format(
                     CredentialUtil.decode(encrypted_credentials))
             }
             response = requests.post(
                 '{}/oauth2/token?grant_type=client_credentials&scope=all'.format(
                     self._client_info.authorization_url),
                 headers=headers,
                 verify=self._verify
             )
             if response.status_code != 200:
                 raise MuseTokenError(
                     'Could not get valid token for Muse API: {}'.format(
                         response.text
                     ))

             result = response.json()
             self._token = result.get('access_token')
             self._token_expired_at = datetime.datetime.now() + datetime.timedelta(
                 seconds=result.get('expires_in')
             )
         except Exception as e:
             raise MuseTokenError(
                 'Could not get valid token for Muse API: {}'.format(e))

     def _check_token(self):
         now = datetime.datetime.now()
         if (not self._token or
                 (self._token_expired_at and now >= self._token_expired_at)):
             self._get_token()

     def _request(self, method, url, **kwargs):
         self._check_token()
         # category_tree
         content_type = kwargs.pop('content_type', 'application/json')
         headers = {
             'Authorization': 'Bearer {}'.format(self._token),
             'Content-Type': content_type,
             'email': self._email,
         }



         max_retries = 5
         base_delay = 2

         for attempt in range(max_retries):
             try:
                 response = requests.request(
                     method,
                     self._client_info.base_url + url,
                     headers=headers,
                     verify=self._verify,
                     **kwargs
                 )

                 # 如果请求成功，跳出重试循环
                 break

             except requests.exceptions.ChunkedEncodingError as e:
                 logger.warning(f'ChunkedEncodingError on attempt {attempt + 1}/{max_retries}: {e}')

                 if attempt < max_retries - 1:
                     # 指数退避策略
                     delay = base_delay * (2 ** attempt)
                     logger.info(f'Retrying in {delay} seconds...')
                     time.sleep(delay)
                     continue
                 else:
                     logger.error('Max retries exceeded for ChunkedEncodingError')
                     raise MuseError(f'Network error after {max_retries} attempts: {e}')

             except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
                 # 其他请求异常不重试，直接抛出
                 logger.error(f'Request failed with non-retryable error: {e}')
                 raise MuseError(f'Request failed: {e}')

         if response.status_code != 200:
             lprint(url, method, kwargs,response, max_length=3800,force_print=True)
             raise MuseError(
                 'Muse API returned invalid response: {}'.format(response.text))

         try:
             result = response.json()
         except Exception as e:
             logger.error(f'Failed to parse JSON response: {e}')
             raise MuseError(
                 'Muse API returned invalid response: {}'.format(response.text))
         lprint(url, method, kwargs,result,max_prints_per_line=40, max_length=1800)
         if result['code'] != 0:
             lprint(url, method, kwargs,result,max_prints_per_line=5, max_length=3800,force_print=True)
             raise MuseError(
                 'Muse API Response Error: {}'.format(result.get('msg', result)))
         #(url, method, kwargs,result['data'],max_prints_per_line=5, max_length=3800)
         return result['data']

     def _get_upload_info(self):
         raise NotImplementedError

     def upload_file(self, file_path, return_info=False):
         """上传文件"""
         if not os.path.exists(file_path):
             raise FileNotFoundError(file_path)

         file_size = os.path.getsize(file_path)
         if not file_size:
             raise ValueError('{} is a empty file, unable to upload'.format(
                 file_path))

         res = self._get_upload_info()
         if file_size < 1024 * 1024 * 1024:
             with open(file_path, 'rb') as f:
                 file_data = f.read()

             result = requests.request(
                 'POST', res['upload_url'],
                 headers={
                     'Authorization': res['token'],
                     'json': 'true',
                 },
                 data=file_data,
                 verify=self._verify
             )

             if result.status_code != 200:
                 raise MuseError(
                     'Muse upload file error: {}, file: {}'.format(
                         result.text, file_path))

             data = result.json()
             if 'url' not in data:  # 💡 upload_file=<function _MuseBase.upload_file at 0x0000029517ECD940> (function)
                 raise MuseError('Muse upload file error: {}, file: {}'.format(
                     data, file_path))

             if not return_info:
                 return result.json()['url']

             _json = result.json()
             _json["log_id"] = res["id"]

             return _json

         # 大文件分片上传
         tus_client = tusclient.client.TusClient(res['upload_url'], headers={
             'Authorization': res['token'],
         })
         logger.debug('Muse upload large file: {}'.format(file_path))

         retry = 0
         while retry < 3:
             try:
                 return self._retry_tus_upload(file_path, tus_client, return_info)
             except Exception as e:
                 retry += 1
                 if retry == 3:
                     raise MuseError(
                         'Muse upload file error: {}，file: {}'.format(
                             e, file_path))

     @staticmethod
     def _retry_tus_upload(file_path, client, return_info=False):
         uploader = client.uploader(file_path, chunk_size=50 * 1024 * 1024)
         uploader.upload()

         if not return_info:
             return uploader.url
         return {'url': uploader.url, 'fsize': uploader.file_size}

     def _format_url(self, data, **kwargs):
         raise NotImplementedError

     def _search_assets(
             self, interface, asset_name=None, category_ids=None, page_size=60,
             page_number=1, query_texts=None,**kwargs):  # ⬅️ (第253行) None

         if not category_ids:
             assert (asset_name or query_texts), 'asset_name or query_texts is required'

         method, url = self._format_url(interface)

         data = {
             'page_num': page_number,
             'page_size': page_size,
         }
         if asset_name:
             data['asset_name'] = asset_name

         if category_ids:
             data['categories'] = category_ids

         if query_texts:
             assert isinstance(query_texts, list), 'query_texts must be a list'
             data['query_texts'] = query_texts

         data.update(kwargs)
         return self._request(method, url, json=data)

     def _redirect_page_detail(self, asset_data):
         method, url = self._format_url(MuseInterface.redirect_page_detail)
         return self._request(method, url, json=asset_data)

     def upload_attachment(self, log_id, file_size, fpurl, file_name, return_info=False):
         method, url = self._format_url(MuseInterface.upload_attachment)

         attachment_info = [
             {
                 "log_id": log_id,
                 "size": file_size,
                 "fpUrl": fpurl,
                 "filename": file_name,
                 "async_task_type": "attachments"
             }
         ]
         result = self._request(method, url, json=attachment_info)
         if return_info:
             return result
         return result[0]["id"]

     def delete_tag_group(self, asset_id, refer_code=None, custom_tags=None, 
                          personal_tags=None, ai_tags=None, refer_type=None):
         """删除资产标签群（自定义标签、个人标签、AI标签）

         :param asset_id: 资产id
         :param refer_code: 资产所属仓库/引用/共享仓库code，默认为organization_id
         :param custom_tags: 自定义标签列表
         :param personal_tags: 个人标签列表
         :param ai_tags: AI标签列表
         :param refer_type: 当资产为共享资产时，必传：referType = 1
         :return: 删除结果，True表示成功，False表示失败
         """
         if not self.organization_id or not self.asset_type:
             raise ValueError('organization_id and asset_type are required')

         # referCode默认为organization（资产在所属仓库操作）
         # 如果资产在引用/共享仓库操作，需要传入正确的referCode
         refer_code = refer_code or self.organization_id

         method, url_template = MuseInterface.delete_tag_group
         url = url_template.format(
             organization=self.organization_id,
             referCode=refer_code,
             assetType=self.asset_type,  # 💡 publish_asset=<function VendorMuseClient.publish_asset at 0x0000029517ECEFC0> (function)
             assetId=asset_id
         )

         params = {}
         if refer_type is not None:
             params['referType'] = refer_type

         if params:  # 💡 get_vendor_spaces=<function VendorMuseClient.get_vendor_spaces at 0x0000029517ECF060> (function)
             url = url + '?' + urlencode(params)

         tag_data = {}  # 💡 set_vendor_space_id=<function VendorMuseClient.set_vendor_space_id at 0x0000029517ECF100> (function)
         tag_types = []
         if custom_tags is not None:
             tag_data['custom_tags'] = custom_tags
             tag_types.append(f"custom_tags({len(custom_tags)})")
         if personal_tags is not None:  # 💡 get_category_tree=<function VendorMuseClient.get_category_tree at 0x0000029517ECF1A0> (function)
             tag_data['personal_tags'] = personal_tags
             tag_types.append(f"personal_tags({len(personal_tags)})")
         if ai_tags is not None:
             tag_data['ai_tags'] = ai_tags
             tag_types.append(f"ai_tags({len(ai_tags)})")


         kwargs = {}
         if tag_data:
             kwargs['json'] = tag_data  # 💡 delete_asset=<function VendorMuseClient.delete_asset at 0x0000029517ECF2E0> (function)

         try:
             result = self._request(method, url, **kwargs)
             return result
         except Exception as e:  # 💡 update_asset=<function VendorMuseClient.update_asset at 0x0000029517ECF380> (function)
             raise
