 # -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
 """
 Muse标签和简介更新异步线程模块
 """
   # 💡 progress_updated=<PySide6.QtCore.Signal object at 0x0000029517DE3910> (Signal)
 import asyncio  # 💡 skip_added=<PySide6.QtCore.Signal object at 0x0000029517DE3850> (Signal)
 import os  # 💡 verify_fail_added=<PySide6.QtCore.Signal object at 0x0000029517DE37F0> (Signal)
 import sys
 import time  # 💡 finished=<PySide6.QtCore.Signal object at 0x0000029517DE3870> (Signal)
 import traceback
 from typing import List, Dict, Any
 from PySide6.QtCore import QThread, Signal

 import muse_python_api
 from muse_python_api.enums import MuseAssetType

 baselibs_path = os.environ.get('BASELIBS_PATH', 
                               os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), '@baselibs'))
 sys.path.insert(0, baselibs_path)
 import Lugwit_Module as LM
 lprint = LM.lprint


 class MuseUpdateTagsThread(QThread):
     """Muse标签和简介更新异步线程"""

     # 信号定义
     progress_updated = Signal(int, str, str, object, str)  # current_index, anim_name, status, is_success, error_msg
     skip_added = Signal(str)  # anim_name
     verify_fail_added = Signal(str)  # anim_name
     finished = Signal(int, int, int, int, list, list)  # success_count, fail_count, skip_count, verify_fail_count, fail_list, verify_fail_list  # 💡 cancel=<function MuseUpdateTagsThread.cancel at 0x0000029517ECF880> (function)
       # ⬅️ (第55行) '<cell at 0x00000295179BFEE0: empty>'
     def __init__(self, parent, anim_data_list: List[Any], config: Dict[str, Any]):
         """
         Args:
             parent: 父对象
             anim_data_list: 动画数据列表（AnimData对象列表）
             config: 配置字典，包含：
                 - email: Muse用户邮箱
                 - organization_id: 组织ID
                 - asset_type_str: 资产类型字符串
                 - config_context: Muse上传配置上下文
                 - refer_code: referCode（可选）
                 - refer_type: referType（可选）
         """
         super().__init__(parent)
         self.anim_data_list = anim_data_list
         self.config = config
         self._cancelled = False

     def cancel(self):
         """取消更新"""
         self._cancelled = True

     def run(self):
         """执行更新任务"""
         try:
             # 获取配置
             email = self.config.get('email')
             organization_id = self.config.get('organization_id')
             asset_type_str = self.config.get('asset_type_str', 'simpleaction')
             config_context = self.config.get('config_context', 'svn/simpleaction_action_sync')
             refer_code = self.config.get('refer_code')
             refer_type = self.config.get('refer_type')
             max_concurrent = 50

             try:
                 asset_type = getattr(MuseAssetType, asset_type_str, MuseAssetType.simpleaction)
             except Exception:
                 asset_type = MuseAssetType.simpleaction

             # 统计信息
             success_count = 0
             verify_fail_count = 0
             fail_count = 0
             fail_list = []
             verify_fail_list = []
             completed_count = 0

             loop = asyncio.new_event_loop()
             asyncio.set_event_loop(loop)

             async def _run_all():
                 semaphore = asyncio.Semaphore(max_concurrent)
                 executor = None  # default executor

                 def _process_one(anim_data: Any) -> Dict[str, Any]:
                     """单个动画的完整更新流程（阻塞函数，放到executor里并发跑）"""
                     if self._cancelled:
                         return {"type": "cancelled", "anim_name": getattr(anim_data, "name", ""), "error": "cancelled"}

                     anim_name = getattr(anim_data, "name", "")
                     tags = anim_data.muse_tags if getattr(anim_data, "muse_tags", None) else []
                     new_tags = list(tags) if tags else []
                     description = getattr(anim_data, "description", "") or ""

                     # 每个任务使用独立 client，避免并发共享导致不稳定
                     client_local = muse_python_api.MuseClient(email=email, organization_id=organization_id, asset_type=asset_type)

                     # 搜索同名资产（不带分类过滤）
                     result = client_local.search_assets(asset_name=anim_name, page_size=200)
                     assets = (result or {}).get("records", []) or []
                     if not assets:
                         return {"type": "fail", "anim_name": anim_name, "error": "未找到资产"}

                     existing_asset = assets[0]
                     asset_id = existing_asset.get("id")
                     asset_organization = existing_asset.get("organization") or organization_id
                     current_refer_code = refer_code if refer_code else asset_organization

                     existing_common = existing_asset.get("common", {}) or {}
                     existing_tags = existing_common.get("custom_tags", []) or []
                     existing_description_multil = existing_asset.get("description_multil", {}) or {}
                     existing_description = existing_description_multil.get("zh_CN", "") if existing_description_multil else ""
                     existing_description_common = (existing_common.get("description", "") or "")

                     desc_match = (existing_description == (description or "")) or (existing_description_common == (description or ""))
                     if set(existing_tags) == set(new_tags) and desc_match:
                         return {"type": "skip", "anim_name": anim_name, "error": ""}

                     # 删除旧标签（尽力而为）
                     old_personal_tags = existing_asset.get("personal_tags", []) or []
                     old_ai_tags = existing_asset.get("ai_tags", []) or []
                     if existing_tags or old_personal_tags or old_ai_tags:
                         try:
                             client_local.delete_tag_group(
                                 asset_id=asset_id,
                                 refer_code=current_refer_code,
                                 custom_tags=existing_tags if existing_tags else None,
                                 personal_tags=old_personal_tags if old_personal_tags else None,
                                 ai_tags=old_ai_tags if old_ai_tags else None,
                                 refer_type=refer_type,
                             )
                             time.sleep(0.3)
                             existing_asset = client_local.get_asset(asset_id)
                             existing_common = (existing_asset.get("common", {}) or {})
                         except Exception:
                             pass

                     update_data = {
                         "common": {
                             **existing_common,
                             "custom_tags": new_tags,
                             # 兼容：部分接口只认 common.description
                             "description": description or "",
                         }
                     }

                     # 保留非 zh_CN 的多语言内容
                     existing_description_multil = existing_asset.get("description_multil", {}) or {}
                     new_description_multil = {k: v for k, v in existing_description_multil.items() if k != "zh_CN"}
                     new_description_multil["zh_CN"] = description or ""
                     update_data["description_multil"] = new_description_multil

                     # 直接使用 client_local.update_asset，避免 muse_uploader 的中间处理可能影响 description 字段
                     client_local.update_asset(asset_id, update_data)

                     # 验证
                     time.sleep(0.3)
                     verify_result = client_local.search_assets(asset_name=anim_name, page_size=200)
                     verify_assets = (verify_result or {}).get("records", []) or []
                     updated_asset = None
                     for a in verify_assets:
                         if a.get("id") == asset_id:
                             updated_asset = a
                             break
                     if not updated_asset:
                         return {"type": "verify_fail", "anim_name": anim_name, "error": "无法找到资产进行验证"}

                     updated_tags = (updated_asset.get("common", {}) or {}).get("custom_tags", []) or []
                     updated_desc_multil = (updated_asset.get("description_multil", {}) or {}).get("zh_CN", "") or ""
                     updated_desc_common = (updated_asset.get("common", {}) or {}).get("description", "") or ""
                     desc_ok = (updated_desc_multil == (description or "")) or (updated_desc_common == (description or ""))
                     if set(updated_tags) == set(new_tags) and desc_ok:
                         return {"type": "success", "anim_name": anim_name, "error": ""}

                     fail_details = []
                     if set(updated_tags) != set(new_tags):
                         fail_details.append("标签不匹配")
                     if not desc_ok:
                         fail_details.append("简介不匹配")
                     return {"type": "verify_fail", "anim_name": anim_name, "error": ",".join(fail_details) if fail_details else "验证失败"}

                 async def _one(idx: int, anim_data: Any):
                     if self._cancelled:
                         return
                     anim_name = getattr(anim_data, "name", "") or "未知动画"

                     async with semaphore:
                         try:
                             result = await loop.run_in_executor(executor, _process_one, anim_data)
                         except Exception as e:
                             result = {"type": "fail", "anim_name": anim_name, "error": str(e)}

                     nonlocal completed_count
                     completed_count += 1
                     current_index = completed_count

                     rtype = result.get("type")
                     err = result.get("error", "") or ""
                     if rtype == "success":
                         nonlocal success_count
                         success_count += 1
                         self.progress_updated.emit(current_index, anim_name, "✓ 更新成功", True, "")
                     elif rtype == "skip":
                         self.skip_added.emit(f"{anim_name}|标签和简介已是最新")
                         self.progress_updated.emit(current_index, anim_name, "⏭ 已跳过（已是最新）", None, "")
                     elif rtype == "verify_fail":
                         nonlocal verify_fail_count
                         verify_fail_count += 1
                         verify_fail_list.append(f"{anim_name} ({err})" if err else anim_name)
                         self.verify_fail_added.emit(anim_name)
                         self.progress_updated.emit(current_index, anim_name, f"⚠ 验证失败: {err}" if err else "⚠ 验证失败", False, err)
                     elif rtype == "cancelled":
                         self.progress_updated.emit(current_index, anim_name, "已取消", None, "cancelled")
                     else:
                         nonlocal fail_count
                         fail_count += 1
                         fail_list.append(f"{anim_name} ({err})" if err else anim_name)
                         self.progress_updated.emit(current_index, anim_name, f"失败: {err}" if err else "失败", False, err)

                 tasks = [_one(i, a) for i, a in enumerate(self.anim_data_list)]
                 await asyncio.gather(*tasks, return_exceptions=True)

             loop.run_until_complete(_run_all())
             loop.close()

             # 发送完成信号（skip_count在主线程中处理，这里传0）
             self.finished.emit(success_count, fail_count, 0, verify_fail_count, fail_list, verify_fail_list)

         except Exception as e:
             lprint(f"[ERROR] 更新线程异常: {str(e)}")
             traceback.print_exc()
             # 发送错误完成信号
             self.finished.emit(0, len(self.anim_data_list), 0, 0, [f"线程异常: {str(e)}"], [])

--- ## 📖 文件格式说明 本文件采用 **Markdown + JSON 索引** 混合格式，支持人类阅读和程序解析。 ### 👤 人类阅读 - 📄 直接查看 Markdown 内容（调用树、详细追踪） - 🔧 使用任何 Markdown 编辑器或查看器 - 🤖 AI 可以理解完整上下文 ### 💻 程序解析 #### 1️⃣ 提取 JSON 索引 
import re, json

# 读取文件
with open("trace.md", "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    content = f.read()

# 提取 JSON 索引
match = re.search(r'<<<JSON_INDEX>>>\s*```json\s*\n(.*?)\n```', content, re.DOTALL)
if match:
    data = json.loads(match.group(1))
    print(f"版本: {data['version']}")
    print(f"总调用: {data['metadata']['total_calls']}")
    print(f"最大深度: {data['metadata']['max_depth']}")
#### 2️⃣ JSON 索引结构（规则驱动格式） 
{
  "version": "2.0",
  "format_version": "2026.03",
  "rules": {
    // 基础配置
    "id_pattern": "call-{seq}",
    "depth_range": [1, 5],
    "slow_threshold": 500,

    // 解析规则
    "parsing": {
      "call_pattern": "callBy\\(深度(\\d+)\\s+路径([\\d\\-]+)\\s+#(\\d+)\\)",
      "func_pattern": "in\\s+(\\w+)\\(\\)",
      "return_pattern": "⬅️\\s*返回值\\s*\\([^)]+\\)\\s*(.+?)(?:\\s*[═\\n]|$)"
    },

    // 组件命名规则
    "components": {
      "call_elements": {
        "call": "lprint-trace-call",
        "code_block": "lprint-trace-code-block"
      },
      "interactive_elements": {
        "ai_button": "ask-ai-code-btn",
        "back_button": "back-to-tree-code-btn"
      }
    },

    // 功能开关
    "features": {
      "enable_params_extraction": true,
      "enable_return_expansion": true
    }
  },
  "metadata": {
    "total_calls": 23,
    "max_depth": 5,
    "generated_at": "2026-03-28T15:20:00Z"
  }
}
